 EPH Patmowtyan ‎fakowlteti Yndhanowr patmowtyan ambioni ( -  owstari) arajin varichy eghel e yndhanowr patmowtyan noragowyn shrjani masnaget profesor Karo Ghazaryany։   t-in ambionr bajhanvowm e erkow masi, steghcvowm en Hin ashxarhi patmatyan & Yndhanowr patmowtyan ambionner։  -  tt. Hin ashxarhi patrimony ambiony ghekavarel e nshanavor mankavarjh-patmaban, hamalsarani bazmamya dasaxos profesor Stepan Nersisyany, isk Nor patmowtyan ambiony՝ evropakan mi qani otar lezowner tirapetogh, HSSH GAA nor patmowtyan lavagowyn masnaget, akademikos Abgar Hovhannisyany։   t. erkow ambionneric kazmavorvel e Yndhanowr patmowtyan ambiony՝ A. Hovhannisyani ghekavarowtyamb։  -  tt. ambiony ghekavarel e profesor Xachik Badalyany, isk  -  tt.` profesor Valter Diloyany։   tvakanic ambioni varich e profesor Albert Stepanyany։   tvakanin ambiony veranvanvel e Hamashxarhayin patmowtyan ambion։ 
 Ambionowm dasavandel en hin ashxarhi patmowtyan lavagowyn masnagetner Stepan Nersisyany & Jhenya Mirzaxanyany, oronq achqi en ynkel dasaxosakan mec varpetowtyamb։ Erkar tariner ambionowm dasavandel en na& docent Nikolay Shahnazaryany, mijnadaraget profesor Howsik Najaryany, nor & noragowyn patmowtyan lavagowyn masnaget, hmowt dasaxos ow mankavarjh docent Marlen Hovhanniasyany, Garegin Harowtyownyany։

 Profesor A. Stepanyani ghekavarowtyamb heghinakneri mi hamaxowmb` Krtowtyan & gitowtyan naxararowtyan patverov, steghcel e hanrakrtakan dproci  - -rd dasaranneri hamashxarhayin patmowtyan dasagrqer։ Drancic «Hin dareri patmowtyowny»& «Nor dareri patmowtyowny»hratarakvel en   tvakanin, isk   tvakanin hratarakvel «Mijin dareri patmowtyowny»& «Noragowyn patmowtyowny»։ Profesor A.  ՙQaghaqakrtowtyownneri tesowtyown & patmowtyown»ararkan dasavandvowm e na& ayl fakowltetneri magistratowrayowm` Romano-germanakan banasirowtyan (Artasahmanyan grakanowtyown), Hogebanowtyan & socologiayi, Ashxarhagrowtyan (Tntesakan ashxarhagrowtyown), Jhowrnalistikayi (Qaghaqakrtowtyownneri tesowtyown & patmowtyown)։ Ancac tasy tarineri yntacqowm Hamashxarhayin patmowtyan ambioni magistratowrayi bovov ancel e showrj qarasown owsanogh։  -y pashtpanel e teknacowakan atenaxosowtyown՝ patmowtyan amenatarber himnaxndirneri veraberyal։ Nrancic erkowsy gitakan astitwan en stacel evropakan hamalsarannerowm։ Errordy ayjhm masnagitanowm e Pekini hamalsaranowm։ 
 Baci planayin dasyntacneric, magistrantneri & bakalavrneri hamar kazmakerpvel en dasaxosowtyownner artasahmanyan gitnakanneri masnakcowtyamb. Qembriji hamalsarani Queen’s College-i dekan profesor T. Braown, Harvardi hamalsarani Hayagitowtyan anbioni varich profesor J. Rassel, Michigani hamalsarani Hayagitowtyan ambioni varich profesor Jh.  Tariner i ver ambioni gitahetazotakan ashxatanqn yntacel e mi qani himnakan owghghowtyownnerov. Minchardyownaberakan, ardyownaberakan & hetardyownaberakan qaghaqakrtowtyownneri himnaharcer, Hayastany Ar&elq-Ar&mowtq qaghaqakrtakan arnchowtyownneri cirowm, Hamashxarhaynacowmy hayoc patmowtyan hamateqstowm, Patmagitakan mitqy & hanrowtayin kyanqy & ayln։  -  tt. ambionowm katarvel e petakan paymanagrayin tema՝ «Haykakan qristoneakan hasarakowtyowny & hay ekeghecin (cagowmnabanowtyowny, hastatowmy & zargacowmy). patmaqnnakan & social-mshakowtayin verlowcowtyown», orowm yndgrkvac en eghel profesor A.Stepanyany & V.Diloyany։ Teman nvirvac e hay qristoneakan ekeghecow cagowmnabanowtyany & haykakan hasarakowtyan mej nra xaghacac derin։ Himnaxndirner, oronq arajnakarg nshanakowtyown ownen hayoc patmowtyan gitakan anachar owsowmnasirowtyan gorcowm։ Ardyownqnery hratarakvel heghinakneri mi sharq hodvacnerowm։ 
 Jhn&i hamalsarani het Evramiowtyan “Research Program in Social Studies” cragri sahmannerowm profesor A.Stepanyany masnakcel e «David the Invincible»temayi katarmany`  -  tvakan-ner։ Nra masnateman er «Neo-Platonic Approach to the Armenian Historiography»։ Cragri gitakan ardyownqneri ampopmamb ayjhm Jhn&i hamalsarany hratarakowm e kolektiv ashxatowtyown, ori he-ghinakneric meky profesor A.Stepanyann e։ 
 Baltimori hamalsarani dramashnorhi shrjanaknerowm profesor A.Stepanyany  -  tva-kannerin masnakcel e «National Identity Alternatives in Multicultural Societies»gitatemayin` «Dimensions of National Identity (Preliminary observations)»։ Dranc ardyownqnery (masamb) ampopvel en nra xmbagrowtyamb   tvakanin lowys tesac «Inqnowtyan harcer»kolektiv ashxatowtyan mej։ Aveli qan   tarineri yntacqowm ambioni andamnery hratarakel en   menagrowtyown &   hodvac։ Gitakan zekowcowmnerov handes en ekel hanrapetakan ow mijazgayin gitajhoghovnerowm` Er&an, Moskva, S.Peterbowrg, Pariz, Varshava, Hrom, Qembrij, Oqsford, Boston, Neapol, Atenq, Salonik & ayln։ 
   tvakanic i ver Tat& gitakrtakan hamaliri hamagorcakcowtyamb ambiony hratarakowm e «Patmowtyown & krtowtyownn»handesy` prof A.Stepanyani xmbagrowtyamb։ Handesi ashxatanqneri masnakcowm en inchpes ambioni, aynpes el hanrapetowtyan twanachvac masnagetnery։ Hratarakvel en dra   hamarnery, hratarakowtyan gorcyntacowm e  / -rd miacyal hamary՝ nvirvac akad. A. Hovhannisyani  -amyakin։ Owsanoghakan gitakan ynkerowtyan gcov «Hamashxarhayin patmowtyown»masnagitacman owsanoghnery  -  tvakannerin hamalsaranakan, hanrapetakan & miowtenakan gitakan konferansnerowm handes en ekel   gitakan zekowcowmnerov, oroncic shatern arjhanacel en mrcanakneri։ 
 Hamashxarhayin patmowtyan ambionowm XSHM-i zanazan qaghaqneric & artasahmanic eghel en stajhorner profesor Al. Egorov (S.Peterbowri hamalsaran), Q. Svering (Sorbon  -rd hamalsaran), profesor S. Dadoyan ( Beyrowt, Amerikyan hamalsaran ), T. ONil (Arizonayi hamalsaran) & aylq։ 
 Ayjhm EPH-i yndhanowr patmowtyan ambionowm ashxatowm e   dasaxos. patmakan gitowtyownneridoktor, profesor Albert Stepanyany, ambioni varich, patmakan gitowtyownneri teknacow, docentner G&org Qilimjyan, Gagik Harowtyownyany, Ervand Margaryany, Hakob Harowtyownyany, Davit Tinoyany, patmakan gitowtyownneri teknacow, asistentner Ara Gasparyany, Smbat Hovhannisyany, asistent Lilit Minasyany։ 
 Jhamavtwari kargov ambionowm ashxatel en patmakan gitowtyownneri doktor, profesor Arman Kirakosyany , banasirakan gitowtyownneri doktor Armanowsh Kozmoyany , banasirakan gitowtyownneri teknacow Sergey Aghajanyany , patmakan gitowtyownneri teknacow, docent Artashes Ghazaryany & aylq։ 
 Girq arajin 
 Yndardak shrjazgesty 
 Chem taqcni, es hatowk bjhshkakan himnarkowtyan hivand em, xnamoghs het&owm e ind, grete achq chi ktrowm indnic, qani or dran vra ka ditancq, isk im xnamakali achqn ayn darchnagowynneric e, oronq ownak chen mijtapanc tesnel ind՝ kapowtachyais։ 
 Het&abar, im hivandapahy erbeq chi karogh linel im tshnamin։ Es nowynisk sireci nran՝ dran et&ic achq dnoghin, & henc na im senyakn e mtnowm, nran zanazan drvagner em patmowm im kyanqic, orpeszi na, chnayac ditancqi xochyndotin, ind aveli lav twanachi։ Amen inchic datelov՝ ayd barin gnahatowm e im patmvacqnery, qanzi heriq e, or es nran hertakan patmowtyowns horinem, na, cankanalov artahaytel ir eraxtagitowtyowny, cowcadrowm e ind ir derqi ashxatanqi hertakan noragowyn nmowshy։ Mi koghm toghnenq ayn harcy, te arvestaget e na, te och։ Chnayac nra steghcac cowcahandesy nowynisk hrapowrel er mi qani gnordneri։ Na hangowycner e hyowsowm sovorakan arasanakic, ory havaqowm, xtwtwvacqic qandowm e hivandasenyaknerowm, aycejhameric heto dranq veracowm bazmahangowyc hreshneri, heto tataxowm gipsi mej, toghnowm, or choranan, & hagcnowm paytya dogherin amracvac gorcelow twagheri vra։ 
 Hatwax na tarvowm e ir steghcagorcowtyownnery gownazardelow gaghaparov։ Es nran et em pahowm ayd mtqic՝ matnacowyc anelov im spitak, laqapat, metaghya mahtwakaly, & xndrowm nran՝ ayd amenakataryal mahtwakaly mtovi patkeracnel gownazard։ Ayd jhamanak na glxaver&owm sarsapov irar e xpowm xnamakali ir derqery՝ miajhamanak pordelov ir poqr֊inch ansharjh demqi vra artahaytel sarsapi bolor hnaravor d&ery & der e qashowm bazmagowyn cragreric։ 
 Ayspisov im petakan, metaghya, spitak laqov patvac mahtwakaly carayowm e orpes chapanish։ Ind hamar ayn nowynisk shat avelin e․ im mahtwakaly՝ da i verjo hasac npatakaket e, im spopanqy, ayn karogh er darnal im havatqy, ete himnarkowtyan tnorinowtyowny towyl tar katarel orosh katarelagorcowmner․ es bardracnel ktayi mahtwakali twaghavandaky, orpeszi ayl&s och oq ind chapic shat chmotenar։ 
 Shabaty mek angam՝ aycelowtyownneri ory, xaxtvowm er im spitak metaghadogherov hyowsvac lrowtyowny։ Ayd jhamanak galis en nranq, ovqer cankanowm en ind prkel, owm hatwowyq e pattwarowm ind sirely, ovqer kowzenayin im mej gnahatel, hargel & twanachel irenq irenc։ Orqan kowyr en nranq, nyardayin, andastirak։ Eghowngneri mkratov qercowm en twaghavandaki spitak laqy, grichnerov ow kapowyt matitnerov erkaravown anparkesht mardowkner en nkarowm։ Im pastabany՝ ir oghjyownov paytecnelov senyaky, amen angam neylone glxarky ccowm e mahtwakalis ormnakoghmi dax syan vra։ Ev twisht aynqan jhamanak, orqan t&owm e nra aycy, ― isk pastabannery karogh en erkar xosel, ― na nman brni gorcoghowtyamb xlowm e im havasarakshrowtyowny & hogow kaytarowtyowny։ 
 Ayn banic heto, erb im aycelownern irenc yncanery i cowyc drecin jranerk hoghmacaghikneri ktavi nerq&owm gtnvogh spitak sprocov seghaniki vra, & ayn banic heto, erb nranc hajoghvec teghekacnel ind im prkowtyann owghghvac՝ irenc yntacik kam cragrvogh gaghaparneri masin & hamozel ind՝ owm nranq aranc hognelow janowm en prkel, merdavori handep irenc siro bardr makardak ownenalow mej, dranov isk krkin irenc goyowtyan hatwowyqn en veragtnowm & lqowm ind։ Heto galis e im xnamoghy՝ odapoxelow & yncaneri patetneri jhapavennery havaqelow։ Hatwax nran eli jhamanak e mnowm, orpeszi odapoxelowc heto nsti im mahtwakalin &, xtwtwvac jhapavennery qandelov, ir showrjy lrowtyown taraci aynqan jhamanak, minch& or es sksowm em lrowtyowny anvanel Browno, isk Brownoyin՝ lrowtyown։ 
 Browno Myownsterbergy, es i nkati ownem xnamoghis & mi koghm em dnowm baraxaghy, im pogherov ind hamar hing haryowr grelatowght e gnel։ Chamowsnacac, erexa chownecogh & armatnerov Zaowerlandic Brownon patrast e, ete pahowsty chbavakanacni, krkin gnal grenakan pitowyqneri poqrik krpak, owr na& mankakan xaghaliqner en vatwarowm, orpeszi ind apahovi gcer chownecogh anhrajhesht makeresov՝ im, howsanq, twshgrit hishoghowtyownneri hamar։ Es erbeq chei karoghana xndrel, or nman carayowtyownner matowcen im aycelownery, asenq, pastabany kam Blepy։ Im nkatmamb hogsashat sery ynkerneris hastat towyl cher ta irenc het berel aynpisi vtangavor mi ban, inchpisin maqowr towghtn e, & ayn tramadrel hogowc andadar dowrs jhaytqogh im xosqerin։ 
 Erb es asaci Brownoyin․ «Ax, Browno, ind hamar hing haryowr tert anmegh towght che՞s gni», na, achqery bardracnelov depi arastagh & hayacqi owghghowtyamb tanelov cowcamaty, patasxanec․ «Dowq nkati owneq spitak to՞wght, paron Oskar»։ 
 Es pndeci im «anmegh» bary & xndreci, or Brownon krpakowm ogtagorci henc da։ Veradarnalov patetov, erekoyan mot, na ashxatec ind tval mtqerov alekocvac Browno։ Bazmativ angam erkar hayacqy pahowm er arastaghi vra, orteghic qaghowm er ir bolor haytnowtyownnery, & qich anc artahaytvec․ «Dowq ind patshatw bar arajarkeciq։ Es ayntegh anmegh towght xndreci, & vatwaroghowhin gowyn tvec֊gowyn arav ow miayn dranic heto katarec im xndranqy»։ Grenakan pitowyqneri xanowtneri vatwaroghowhineri masin erkarat& zrowycic xowsapelov՝ es zghjaci, or towghtn anmegh em anvanel, isk heto lreci՝ spaselov minch& Brownon dowrs ga senyakic & miayn dranic heto baceci hing haryowr towght parownakogh patety։ 
 Twkown chentarkvogh patetn im derqowm erkar chpaheci & canrowtet& chareci։ Es hashveci tasy tert, mnacacy taqcreci mahtwakali seghaniki darakowm, inqnahosy haytnabereci arkghowm՝ lowsankarneri albomi koghqin։ Grichy licqavorvac e, tanaqi pakasowtyown chi karogh linel, bayc inchpe՞s sksem։ 
 Cankowtyan depqowm patmowtyowny kareli e sksel mejteghic &, xizaxoren araj kam et sharjhvelov, bolorin shpotecnel։ Kareli e ashxatel modernisti otwov․ merjhel bolor jhamanaknery & taracowtyownnery՝ heto haytnaberelow hamar, or henc nor i verjo qez hajoghvec lowcel taracowtyan & jhamanaki xndiry։ Kareli e henc arajin ejeric haytararel na&, or mer orerowm yndhanrapes hnaravor che vep grel, oric heto henc sepakan heghinakowtyownd qez tikownq dardrac՝ mi hzor gorc nerkayacnes & ardyownqowm orpes verjin yndowneli vipasan handes gas։ Es towyl ktayi ind na& asel, or hamest e hnchowm, erb dow, orpes skizb, haytararowm es, te ayl&s chkan vipayin herosner, qani or ayl&s chkan anhatakanowtyownner, qani or anhatakanowtyownn anveradard korsvac e, qani or mardy miaynak e, yowraqanchyowry havasarapes miaynak e & anhatakan miaynakowtyan iravownq chowni & miaxarnvowm e ananown ow herosakanowtyownic zowrk miatarr amboxin։ Ter&s da aydpes el e & owni ir himnavorowmy։ Sakayn inch veraberowm e ind՝ Oskaris & im xnamoghin՝ Brownoyin, kcankanayi haytararel․ menq erkowss el herosner enq, bacardakapes tarber herosner enq․ na՝ ditancqi ayn koghmowm, es՝ ancqi dimac, & nowynisk erb na bacowm e dowry, menq erkowss, mer arac ynkerowtyamb ow mer miaynakowtyamb handerd, amen&in el ananown, herosakanowtyownic zowrk amboxi chenq veracvowm։ 
 Es sksowm em aveli vagh jhamanakic, qani or och oq chi hamardakvi nkaragrel im kyanqy, ete bavakanachap hamberowtyown chowni, orpeszi, naxqan sepakan kecowtyan darashrjany naxagcely, chhishataki ir paperi ow tateri gone kesin։ De, owremn, towyl tveq ind dez bolorid՝ im ynkernerin & im amenshabatya aycelownerin, or im bjhshkakan himnarkowtyan pateric dowrs gtnvelov՝ stipvac en aprel xarnashpot kyanqov, dez bolorid, or nowynisk kaskacner el chowneq gratghti vra arvac im grarowmneri masin, nerkayacnel Oskari morakan tatikin։ 
 Anna Bronski anownov im taty hoktemberyan mi orva avartin nstac er kartofili dashti ezrin։ Hoghin nstac er henc shrjazgestnerov։ Naxqan twashi jhamy kareli er het&el, te inchpes e tats hmtoren pocxowm taramac ter&nery՝ xnamqov dasavorelov xmberi, twashin mot na kerav osharaki mej qaghcracrac mi ktor twarpot hac, aynowhet& verjin angam qaghhanec dashty & verjapes ir shrjazgestnerov nstec erkow grete berneberan lcvac koghovneri mij&։ Qterov mimyanc owghghvac nra erkaratwit koshikneri nerbanneri koghqin cxowm er ter&neri poqrik xarowyky՝ erbemn astmatikoren kendananalov & cowxy janasirabar araqelov haziv nkateli teqowtyown ownecogh erkrakegh&n i var։ Innsowniny tivn er, isk tats nstac er Kashowbyan erkramasi henc srtowm, Bisaowic och herow, & el aveli mot Ramqaowi dimaci aghyowsi gorcaranin, Fireqic ayn koghm, ortegh Dirshaowi & Qarthaowsi mij& ynkac mayrowghin tanowm er depi Brentaow։ Nstac er tikownqov depi s& Holdqrowg antary & ayrvac ynkowzenow ayrvac twyowghi cayrov kartofilnery hrowm er taq moxri tak։ 
 Ete es henc nor hatowk hishatakeci im tatiki shrjazgesty, karcowm em՝ liovin hstak asaci․ «Na nstac er ir shrjazgestnerov» & na& grqis ays glowxn anvaneci «Yndardak shrjazgest», nshanakowm e՝ gitem, te inchov em es partakan ayd hagowstin։ Im taty mek shrjazgest cher krowm, ayl՝ amboghj chorsy՝ meky myowsi vra։ Ynd orowm, na och te krowm er mek verin & ereq nerqin shrjazgestner, och, na krowm er chors, ayspes kochvac, verinner, amen mi shrjazgest ir vra krowm er hajordin։ Tats chors shrjazgestnery krowm er oroshaki hamakargov, hamadayn ori՝ dranc hajordakanowtyownn orecor poxvowm er։ Ayn, inch erek hagac er amenaver&ic, aysor gtnvowm er ayd ver&ini anmijapes taky, erkrord shrjazgesty darnowm er errordy։ Erekva errord shrjazgestn aysor anmijakanoren hpvowm er marmnin, isk shrjazgesty, orn erek amenamotn er marmnin, aysor cowcadrowm er ir naxshery, aveli twisht՝ dranc bacakayowtyowny․ Anna Bronski anownov im tatiki bolor shrjazgestnery naxyntrowm ein mek & mi&nowyn՝ kartofili gowyny։ Ayd gowyny petq e or nran sazer։ 
 Tatikis shrjazgestnery, gowynic baci, arandnanowm ein ktori artaroc chaperov։ Dranq mert kloranowm ein, pont ein talis, erb pchowm er qamin, & kax ein ynknowm, erb qamin bacakayowm er, cacanvowm ein, erb ayn koghqov er ancnowm, & bolor chorsy titerneri pes trchowm ein tatikis arj&owm, erb qamin pchowm er tikownqic։ Isk nstelis na ir bolor shrjazgestnery havaqowm er ir taky։ 
 Chors mshtapes owrac, taramac, calqerov vayr ijnogh kam datark cci pes mahtwakali koghqin kangnac shrjazgestneric baci tats owner na& hingerordy։ Ayd hingerordy oroshakioren ochnchov cher tarbervowm mnacac chors kartofilagowynneric։ Ynd orowm, och misht er, or orpes hingerord shrjazgest mek & mi&nowyn shrjazgestn er carayowm։ Ir eghbayrakicneri pes, qanzi shrjazgestnery ojhtvac en tghamardkayin bnavorowtyamb, na &s entaka er poxarinman, mtnowm er chors hagnvoghneri tvi mej։ Mnacac shrjazgestneri nman, erb galis er ir herty՝ aysinqn՝ amen hingerord owrbat gnowm er owghigh depi tashtaky։ Shabat orerin kaxvowm er xohanoci patowhani demi paranin, isk heto haytnvowm ardowki taxtaki vra։ 
 Erb tats aydpisi maqra֊naxapatrasta֊ardowkayin shabat orerin, kovy ktelowc ow kerakrelowc heto, amboghjapes xorasowzvowm er tashtakayin gorceri mej, otwarayin inch֊or ban er haghordowm, aynowhet& jowry krkin tapowm, orpeszi caghkavor savani mej parowrvac nsti ankoghnow cayrin՝ ir arj&owm prvac chors hagnvogh & mek tarm lvacac shrjazgestneri dimac։ Tats aj derqi cowcamaty henowm er aj achqi honqi nerq&i masin & och meki xorhowrdy cher lsowm, nowynisk ir eghbayr Vincenti & ayd isk pattwarov arag oroshowm er kayacnowm։ Otabobik kangnac, na otqeri matnerov mi koghm er hrowm ayn shrjazgesty, ory mnacacneric aravel er korcrel kartofili gowyni payly, isk azatvac teghy zbaghecnowm er tarm lvacacy։ 
 I pars Hisowsi, owm masin tats owner hstak patkeracowmner, kiraki aravotyan Ramqaowi ekegheci owgh&orvelow hamar na tarmacnowm er shrjazgestneri hajordakanowtyowny։ Isk e՞rb er tats krowm lvacac shrjazgesty։ Na och miayn maqraser, ayl& snapar kin er, ayd isk pattwarov lavagowyn shrjazgesty cowcadrabar krowm er lav eghanakin, ar&in։ 
 Erkowshabti kesoric heto er, erb im taty nstac er ir xarowyki mot, ori mej xorovvowm er kartofily, kiraknorya shrjazgesty dardel er iren mek shertov aveli mot, isk ayn shrjazgesty, ory kiraki ory taqanowm er nra mashki jermowtyamb, erkowshabti ory՝ havowr patshatwi, xamrac tesqov grkel er nra azdrery։ Tats inch֊or ban er sowlowm, bayc och erg & miajhamanak kaghne caxi moxri mijic dowrs er qashowm arajin xorovvac kartofily։ Kartofily tats drec mi koghm, cxacogh ter&neri mot, orpeszi qamin karoghana ayn sarecnel։ Aynowhet& sowr twyowghy cakec poqr֊inch ayrvac, kegh&y paytac kartofili patary, & tats ayn motecrec beranin & dadarec sowlel։ Dra poxaren na sksec pchelov maqrel moxirn ow hoghy twaqtwqac showrteri aranqowm seghmvac kegh&i vrayic։ Ayd pahin tatiks kkocec achqery։ Heto miayn, oroshelov, or pchel maqrel e orqan harkn e, na bacec nax mek, heto myows achqy, kcec kartofily nosr ktrichnerov, krkin dadarec atamnerov seghmel։ Alyowrashat & chapazanc taq ow golorshi ardakogh kartofili kesy pahelov bac berani mej, tats kloracac achqerov nayowm er minch& horizonn ynkac dashtin, ayn hatogh heragrasyownerin ow aghyowsi gorcarani cxnelowyzi verin masin։ 
 Heragrasyowneri aranqowm inch֊or ban er sharjhvowm։ Tatiks pakec berany, seghmec showrtery, kkocec achqery & camec kartofily։ Inch֊or ban er sharjhvowm heragrasyowneri aranqowm։ Inch֊or ban catkec ayntegh։ Ereq tghamard catkecin depi cxnelowyzy, heto vazqov ancan nra dimacic, isk meky՝ tesqic kartw ow hastlik, shrjvec & arag vazqov krkin ktrec ancav darsac aghyowsneri sharqeri mijov, isk erkow owrishner՝ nihar ow bardrahasak, och aranc djhvarowtyan ancan aghyowsneri mijov ow krkin arag vazecin syowneri aranqov։ Hastlikn ow kartwliky napastaki pes olor֊molor vazowm er & aknhaytoren aveli shat er shtapowm, qan niharnery, & verjinnery stipvac ein krkin netvel cxnelowyzi koghmy, orovhet& kartwlikn arden ancel er nra mijov, minch irenq der miayn aragowtyown ein havaqowm։ Hankarc nranq anhetacan՝ ases mtqapox eghan, & kartwliky, catkelov cxnelowyzic, ynkav horizonic ayn koghm։ 
 Nranq bolorn ayntegh mnacin & yndmijowm tvecin kam, hnaravor e, zgestapoxvecin, kam sksecin sharel tarm aghyowsnery՝ dra hamar vtwar stanalov։ 
 Isk erb im taty cankacav ogtvel yndmijowmic & tweghqel erkrord kartofily, na vripec։ Orovhet& na, ory hastlik er ow kartwlik, nowyn tesqov haytnevec horizoni vra՝ er&i te erkow hetapndoghnerin toghnelov cankapati ayn koghmowm, aghyowsneri kam Brenaow tanogh kamrji mot։ Na ancav ays koghm, sakayn, mi&nowyn e, shat er shtapowm, owzowm er hasnel & et&owm toghnel heraxosasyownery, erkar, dandaghecvac catkelov dashti mijov, aynpes or nra otqeric ays ow ayn koghm ein trchowm cexi ktorner, isk inqy andamb ayd cexic mi koghm er trchowm & inchpes or tapov er trchowm, ayd nowyn hamarowtyamb el ancnowm er kavi vrayov։ Erbemn tvowm er, te na ansharjhanowm e odi mej, twisht aynqan, orqan jhamanaky nran kbavarari։ Kartwliky srbec twakaty, naxqan mi otqov krkin ayd tarm herkac hoghin henvely, orn ir bolor akosneri & kartofili ir hing kowyteri het miasin glorvec depi dorak։ 
 Ev kartwliky hasav dorakin, sakayn ayntegh el anhetacav, erb nihar ow bardrahasak erkow myowsnery, oronq havanabar ayd jhamanakahatvacowm hascrel ein znnel aghyowsi gorcarani nersy, nownpes maglcecin & ancan horizoni gicy։ Nranq sksecin xrvel kavi mej, inchi pattwarov im taty krkin chkaroghacav tweghqel kartofily, orovhet& amen or che, or kareli e tesnel, te inchpes ereq chapahas mardik, tarber boyeri, vazowm en heragrasyowneri mijov & qich e mnowm kotren aghyowsi gorcarani cxnelowyzy։ 
 Heto meky myowsi het&ic՝ nowyn djhvarowtyamb, krownkneri vra aveli ow aveli shat kav qarsh talov, catkotowm en Vincenti erkow or araj herkac dashti mijov ow anhetanowm doraki mej։ 
 Showtov bolor ereqy anhetacan, & im tatiky verjapes karogh er shownch qashel & tweghqel arden grete sarac kartofily։ Na anpowtoren maqrec kegh&i miayn hoghn ow moxiry, kartofiln amboghjowtyamb mtcrec berany & mtacec (ete kareli e aydpes asel), or ayd ereqy er&i te aghyowsagorcner ein։ Tats sksec sharjhel cnoty, erb meky dowrs trav dorakic, s& begheric ver paylowm ein vayri achqery, erkow catkov haytnvec xarowyki mot, des ow den netvec, hayhoyec, vaxic doghac, chgiter owr paxchi․ et chi kareli, orovhet& et&owm dorakic motenowm ein nihar ow barak ayn erkowsy։ Na ynkav cnkneri vra, & nra achqery qich mnac dowrs trchen bneric, & twakatin qrtinq tvec։ Xeghdvelov, doghacogh beranov, na soghac aveli mot, hasav tatis nerbannerin, inchpes mi poqrik gazan՝ nayec nran, aynpes, or tats hogoc hanec, dadarec camel, nerbannery ijecrec getnin, ayl&s chmtacelov o՛ch gorcarani, o՛ch aghyowsneri, o՛ch darsoghneri masin, ayl owghghaki bardracrec shrjazgesty, och, miangamic bolor chorsy։ Bardracrec aynqan, or kartwliky karoghanar clkel dranc tak, bolor chorsi tak։ Ev na anhetacav ir begheri het mektegh & ayl&s nman cher gazani։ Na Ramqaowic cher & och el Fireqic, ayl՝ ir sarsapi het mektegh, shrjazgesti tak er & ayl&s cnkneri vra cher ynknowm։ Kartwliky zbaghecrec ir teghy, moracav doghi masin, & lrowtyown tirec։ Inchpes naxord ory towyl qamin xaghowm er ter&owqi mej, heraxosasyownern ases mimyanc dayn ein talis, aghyowsi gorcarani cxnelowyznery veradardan skzbnakan dirqin, isk im taty, erkrordi vrayov xohemabar hartec arajin shrjazgesty, heto chorrordy & nor errordy & och mi kerp cher karoghanowm haskanal, te inch nor ow zarmanali ban e katarvowm ayntegh՝ ir mashki het։ Da zarmanali er, chnayac ver&owm amen inch miangamayn barevayelowch er։ Tats moxri mijic dowrs qashec erkow֊ereq kartofil, aj armownki taki zambyowghic hanec chors howm kartofil, dranq hertov mek ar mek, mtcrec taq moxri mej, ver&ic el taq moxir avelacrec & xarnec, inchic xarowyky krkin sksec cxal՝ el i՞nch er mnowm nran anel։ 
 Sakayn henc nor ein tatikis shrjazgestnery hangstacel, henc nor er na nexac ter&neri xit cowxy dardyal owghghel depi harav֊ar&mowtq, erb dorakic dowrs prcan nihar ow bardrahasak ayn erkowsy, oronq hetapndowm ein kartwlikin, ory nerkayowms kenowm er shrjazgestneri tak։ Parzvec, or nihar ow bardrahasaknery, yst carayowtyan patkanelowtyan, krowm en dashtayin ostikanowtyan hamazgest։ 
 Nranq pampowshti pes slacan tatis motov։ Karces nrancic meky trav xarowyki vrayov։ Sakayn nranq hankarcaki owshqi ekan, argelakecin irenc erkaratwit koshikneri krownknerov, shrjvecin, koshiknerov dopecin, heto haytnvecin cxi mej։ Hazalov, nranq hamazgestnern azatecin cxic &, cowxy tanelov irenc het&ic, xosakcowtyown sksecin im tatiki het։ Nranq hetaqrqrvecin, te chi՞ tesel na ardyoq, Kolyachekin, qani or anpayman petq e tesac liner nran՝ nstac linelov aystegh՝ doraki mot։ Kolyacheky henc dorakov heracav։ 
 Im tatiky och mi Kolyachek cher tesel, orovhet& och mi Kolyacheki chi twanachowm։ Na harcrec, te aghyowsi gorcaranic chi՞ ardyoq na patahabar, qani or aynteghi ashxatoghneric baci inqy owrishnein chgiti։ Hamazgestavornery nran nkaragrecin Kolyachekin՝ mardow, orn aghyowsi gorcarani het kap chowni, isk artaqnapes kartw e ow hastlik։ Tats hishec, or karces te tesel e, te inchpes aydpisi mekn aysteghov vazec & sowr osti vra xrac cxacogh kartofilov cowyc tvec paxowsti owghghowtyowny depi Bisaow։ Ete havatanq kartofilin, ayn ynkac er gorcaranic hashvac, vecerord ow yoterord syowneri mij&։ Sakayn ayd vazoghy Kolyachekn er, te och՝ im tatiky chgiter, na neroghowtyown xndrec ir anteghyakowtyan hamar՝ meghqy gcelov cxacogh xarowyki vra։ Hogsy shat e, xarowykn el haziv e ayrvowm, aha te inchow nran chen hetaqrqrowm mardik, oronc inqy chi twanachowm։ Na giti miayn nranc, ovqer Bisaowic, Ramaqowic, Fireqic en kam aghyowsi gorcaranic, iren da el bavarar e։ 
 Aselov ays xosqery tats hogoc hanec tet&aki, sakayn bavakanachap bardr, aynpes or hamazgestavornery hetaqrqrvecin, te inchn e nra hogoci pattwary։ Na glxi sharjhowmov cowyc tvec depi xarowyky, ibr hogoc e hanowm towyl kraki hamar & mi qich el՝ cxi miji mardkanc hamar։ Heto na՝ ir sakavativ ktrichnerov kcelov kartofili kesy, amboghjapes trvec camelown, isk achqeri xndoraknery tarav depi ver ow dax։ 
 Dashtayin ostikanowtyan hamazgestavornery hastatapes chein karoghanowm haskanal tatis antarber hayacqy, chgitein՝ arjhe՞, ardyoq, pntrel heraxosasyowneric ayn koghm Bisaowi owghghowtyamb & ayd pattwarov jhamanak ar jhamanak irenc karabinnerov xpowm ein koghqy gtnvogh der chayrvac ter&owqi kowyterin։ Aynowhet&՝ het&elov hankarcahas mghowmin, miangamic showr tvecin erkow li koghovnery, oronq drvac ein tati armownkneri tak, & och mi kerp chein karoghanowm haskanal, te inchow koghovneric irenc otqeri tak glorvecin bacarapes kartofilner, & och mi Kolyachek։ Anvstahowtyamb lcvac, nranq ancan kartofili cghotov cackvac kowyteri mijov, karces Kolyacheky karogh er aydqan kartw jhamanakahatvacowm cackvel dmerva hamar naxapatrastac cghotov, nranq arden xpowm ein npatakaowghghvac, sakayn aydpes el och mi twich chlsecin։ Nranc kaskacnern owghghvac ein nowynisk depi amenaxghtwowk towpy, yowraqanchyowr mkan bniky, depi kowghberi tmbery & krkin ow krkin՝ depi im taty, ory nstel er karces ayd teghin sertatwac, ax ow vax er anowm, pttowm er achqery, sakayn aynpes, or spitakowcy mna tesaneli, tvarkowm er kashowbaci bolor srberi anownnery, sakayn towyl cxacogh xarowyky & showr tvac erkow zambyowghnery haziv te karoghanayin bacatrel nra chapic dowrs oghbali & chapic dowrs bardr hogocnery։ 
 Hamazgestavornery mot kes jhamic och pakas mnacin tatiki koghqin kangnac։ Erbemn nranq kangnowm ein qich hervowm, erbemn krakin aveli mot, achqachapov motavorapes hashvarkowm ein minch aghyowsi gorcarani cxnelowyzy ynkac taracowtyowny, owzowm ein grohel na& Bisaown, sakayn hetadgecin hardakowmy։ Nranq kraki vra pahecin kisakaptac derqery, minch& chstacan im tatikic, ory naxkini pes anyndhat hogoc er hanowm, yowraqanchyowry mekakan twaqac kartofil paytiki vra։ Sakayn camelow gorcyntaci jhamanak hamazgestavornery mtaberecin, or hamazgestner en krowm & dashti mijov vazecin doraki ezri orotwi coghownneri aranqov, vaxecrin napastakin, ory nowynpes Kolyachek cher։ Kraki mot nranq krkin haytnaberecin alyowrot taq golorshi ardakogh kartofilner &, xaghaghasirowtyownic drdvac, oroshaki nerqin dimadrowtyowny haghtaharelov, oroshowm yndownecin howm kartofilnery krkin et gcel koghovneri mej, oronc shrjely irenc partqn er eghel։ 
 Miayn erb erekon hoktemberyan erknqic teghac barak, shegh andr&y, & ijav tanaqagowyn aghjamowghjy, nranq anshtap & aranc or&e cankowtyan hardakowm gorcecin hervowm՝ xavari mej owrvagcvogh mi jhayraqari vra, sakayn ayd hardakowmic heto hrajharvecin hetaga porderic։ Eli mi kartw jhamanak otqic otq poxvelov՝ derqery orhnanqi sharjhowmov pahecin amen owghghowtyamb cowx ardakogh xarowyki vra, eli hazacin kanach cxic, deghin cxic achqery lcvecin artasowqov, apa՝ hazocov ow arcownqnerov, twtqakoshiknern owghghecin depi Bisaow։ Qani or Kolyacheky aystegh che, nshanakowm e Bisaowowm e։ Dashtayin ostikannery mshtapes giten miayn erkow hnaravorowtyown։ 
 Dandagh mahacogh kraki cowxy parowrec im tatikin՝ ases orpes hingerord shrjazgest՝ ayn astitwan yndardak, or taty՝ hogocnerov & bolor srberi anownnery showrterin, nowynpes haytnvec ir chors shrjazgestneri tak, inchpes Kolyacheky։ Miayn erb hamazgestavornery veracvecin hervowm trchkotogh keteri, oronq dandagh heranowm en depi heraxosasyowneri mij& ynkac erekon, tatiky otqi kangnec։ Ayn el aynpisi djhvarowtyamb, karces ayd jhamanakahatvacowm hascrel er armatner gcel, isk ayjhm ir et&ic tanelov armatnery & hoghagndery, ases yndhatowm er dranc nor sksac atwy։ 
 Kolyacheky sksec mrsel, erb anspaselioren ir cackocic zrkvac, haytnvec andr&i tak՝ kartwlik ow hast։ Na showtapowyt kotwkec shalvary, ori bacvely teladrvac er mec vaxov & taqstoc mtnelow ansahman pahanjov։ Shat arag sarchelowc zgowshanalov՝ na matnerov hapshatap vazec kotwakneri vrayov, qani or nman eghanakin heshtic el hesht e ashnanayin mrsacowtyown derq berel։ 
 Im taty moxri tak haytnaberec &s chors taq kartofil։ Drancic ereqy na tvec Kolyachekin, meky inqy kcec & eli harcrec՝ ardo՞q aghyowsi gorcaranic che ayd mardy, te& karogh er arden haskacac linel, or Kolyacheky haytnvel e och aghyowsi gorcaranic, ayl mek owrish teghic։ Heto na, owshadrowtyown chdardnelov verjini patasxani vra, nra vra drec aveli tet& koghovy, isk inqy kqvec ayn meki tak, orn aveli canr er։ Tati mi derqy azat mnac pocxeri & brichi hamar, & na, ir chors shrjazgestneri mej koghovy, kartofily, pocxery & brichy tap talov, sharjhvec Bisaow֊Abbaowi owghghowtyamb։ Yst eowtyan da bown Bisaown cher։ Da aveli showt Ramqaowi owghghowtyown er։ Aghyowsi gorcarany mnac dax koghmowm, isk irenq sharjhvecin depi s& antary, ortegh gtnvowm er Goldkrowgy, & heto arden galis er Brentaown։ Sakayn antari dimaci dorakowm el ynkac er Bisaow֊Abbaown։ Henc aystegh el im tati et&ic gnac kartwlik ow hast Yozef Kolyacheky, orn ayl&s cher karogh bajhanvel chors shrjazgestneric։ 
 Lasti tak 
 Amen&in hesht che aystegh՝ Brownoyi achqov zinvac apake ditancqi nshanarowtyan tak, hatowk bjhshkakan himnarkowtyan՝ otwarov lvacvac, metaghya mahtwakali vra parkac verartadrel kashowbyan ayrvogh ter&neri taki cxi eriznery & hoktemberyan andr&i cancy։ Ete mots chliner im tmbowky, ory, hmowt & hamberatar verabermownqi depqowm, erkrordakan manrowqneric kverhishi amen anhrajheshty՝ tghti vra glxavory artacolelow hamar, & ete es chownenayi himnarkowtyan towyltvowtyownn ar ayn, or orakan ereqic chors jham karogh em xosqy tramadrel im titeghatowpin, es klinei djhbaxt mard՝ aranc pastaci hastatvac tati ow papi։ 
 Amen depqowm im tmbowkn asowm e․ innsowniny tvi ayn hoktemberyan ory, erb qeri Kryowgery Haravayin Amerikayowm xozanaki ognowtyamb pomposhacnowm er tpowtneri nmanvogh ir anglatyac honqery, Dirshaowi & Karthaowsi motakayqowm, Bisaowi aghyowsi gorcaranic och herow՝ chors miagowyn shrjazgestneri tak, xeghdogh cxi, vaxeri, tnqocneri mej, shegh andr&i & srberi bardragowyn hishatakman owghekcowtyamb, towlamit harcowporderi & erkow dashtayin ostikanneri cxov patvac hayacqneri nerqo kartwlik, bayc hast Yozef Kolyacheky saghmnavorec im mory՝ Agnesin։ Anna Bronskin, im taty, ayd gisherva s& cackoci tak hascrec na& poxel anowny․ na towyl tvec, orpeszi sowrb yncanery shrayloren msxogh vanakani janqerov iren veranvanen Anna Kolyachek & ir Yozefi het gnac togh or och Egiptos, bayc gavari kentronakan qaghaqy՝ Motlaow geti vra, ortegh Yozefy gtav lastavari ashxatanq &, orosh jhamanakov, apastan ostikanneric։ 
 Miayn ayn mitowmov, orpeszi orosh chap mecacnem larowmy, arayjhm chem talis Motlaowi getaberanowm teghakayvac qaghaqi anowny՝ chnayac ayn miangamayn arjhani e hishatakman՝ arnvazn orpes mi vayr, ortegh cnvec im mayriky։ Erb zro֊zro tvi howlisi verjin mot՝ henc ayd jhamanak, yndownvec razmakan navatormi shinararowtyan kayserakan cragiry krknapatkelow oroshowmy՝ Aryowci kendanakerpi tak lowys ashxarh ekav im mayriky։ Ir handep havat & erazkotowtyown, mecahogowtyown & paramolowtyown։ Arajin towny, orn anvanowm ein na& Domus vitae, [ ] naxnineri kendanakerpi tak՝ dyowrazgac dkner։ 
 Aregaki ynddimadir linely Neptowni handep, inchpes na& yoterord towny՝ Somus matrimonil uxoris [ ] bardowtyownner ein xostanowm։ Veneran ynddimowtyan mej e Satowrni handep, ory, orqanov haytni e, berowm e lyardi ow paycaghi hivandowtyown, anvanvowm e «ttow» molorak, orn ishxowm e Ayceghjyowrowm & partowtyowny tonowm՝ Aryowcowm, ory Neptownin odadkner e hyowrasirowm, isk poxareny՝ kowghb stanowm, ory sirowm e baleni, sox, twakndegh & lava e artanetowm, isk ginin ttvacnowm e։ Venerayi het hamategh na kenowm er owterord tany, mahvan tany, djhbaxtowtyan masin mtqer er nershnchowm, ayn jhamanak, erb kartofili dashtowm beghnavorowmy xostanowm er azgakanneri tany handgnowtyan astitwani erjankowtyown՝ Merkowrii hovanavorowtyan nerqo։ 
 Aystegh es petq e nerkayacnem mayrikis boghoqy, ov bolor jhamanaknerowm vtwrakanoren jhxtowm er, or saghmnavorvel e kartofili dashtowm։ Twisht e, na yndownowm er, or ir hayry der ayntegh naxadernec arajin pordery, sakayn nra bown vitwaky, inchpes na& Anna Bronskow brnac dirqy, chapazanc anhajogh ein yntrvac, orpeszi Kolyacheki hamar steghcen beghmnavorman hamar anhrajhesht paymanner։ 
 «Da petq e or teghi ownecac liner paxowsti gishery kam Vincent qerow sayli vra, kam verjapes Troilowm, erb menq dowlagocneri mot apastan gtanq»։ 
 Ayspisi xosqerov er mayriks sovorabar himnavorowm ir cagman tvagrowmy, & tatiks, ory da aveli lav petq e gitenar, hezoren glxov er anowm & haytnowm ashxarhin․ «Iharke, poqriks, dow twisht es, ka֊chka da sayli vra e eghel kam verjapes Troilowm, miayn te och dashtowm․ ayd jhamanak &՛ qami er pchowm, &՛ andr& er tapvowm inchpes dowylic»։ 
 Vincenty tatikis eghbayrn er։ Knoj vagh mahvanic heto na owxtagnacowtyown katarec depi Chenshtoxalow & Chenshtoxovyan Mataka Boskan kargadrec nran՝ iren orpes Lehastani apaga tagowhi twanachel։ 
 Ayd jhamanakic i ver Vincenty zbaghvac er miayn nranov, or porprowm er artasovor grqery՝ yowraqanchyowr artahaytowtyan mej gtnelov Lehakan gahin Astvacamor iravownqneri hastatowmy՝ ir qrojy toghnelov tnamerdi & dashti bolor hogsery։ Vincenti ordin՝ Yany, orn ayd jhamanak chors tarekan er, towlakazm, lackan erexa, sagerin er aracacnowm, havaqowm xaytabghet nkarner &, zarmanalioren vagh, postayin droshmanishner։ 
 Aha henc ayd townn er, orn orhnvac er Lehastani erknayin tagowhow koghmic, & owr tatiks hascrec kartofilov li zambyowghnery, & dra het miasin՝ Kolyaychekin։ Vincenty &s imacav, te inch e teghi ownecel, isk imanalov՝ slacav depi Ramqaow & ayntegh sksec tmbkaharel notari dowry, orpeszi na, zinveloov ir sowrb yncanerov, dowrs gar & nshaner kowys Anna Yozefin։ Der cher hascrel Astco qnatatax spasavorn anel ir orhnowtyowny, ory chapic dowrs erkarec ansandeli horanji pattwarov, &, parg&atrvelov xozatwarpi lav patarov, handisatesneri koghmy shrjel ir sowrb tikownqy, erb Vincenty lcec ir zambiky & norapsaknerin teghavorec cghoti ow datark parkeri vra։ Mrsac ow tnktnkacogh Yanin nstecrec ir koghqy, atoraki vra, oric heto diown haskacrec, or gna՝ och mi tegh chteqvelov, owghigh depi gishery․ norapsaknery shtapowm ein։ 
 Der&s mowt, sakayn arden bavakanachap nahanjogh gisherva mijov mer owgh&ornery hasan payti navahangist, ory gtnvowm er gavari kentronakan qaghaqowm։ Ynkernery, oronq Kolyaycheki nman lastaraqichner ein, yndownecin paxstakan zowygin։ Vincenty karogh er ir din shrjel ow qshel et՝ depi Bisaow, kovy, aycy, xozy՝ ir xotwkornerov, sagery & baki showny spasowm ein, te erb ker khascnen irenc, isk ordi Yany petq e parkecver ankoghin, orovhet& jermowtyown owner։ 
 Kolyaycheky taqnvec ereq shabat, isk mazery sovorecrec ayl sanrvacqi՝ mejteghi bacvacqov, saprec beghery, derq berec anteri pastatghter & Yozef Vranka anvamb stacav lastavari ashxatanq։ Isk incho՞w Kolyaychekin hark eghav antaravatwarnerin & payti sghocaranneri tererin nerkayacnel Vrankayi anownov grvac pastatghtery՝ mard, orin ceckrtowki jhamanak lastic cac ein netel Modlin bnakavayri mot՝ Bowg geti nerqin hosanqowm, inchic teghyak cher ghekavarowtyowny։ Bann ayn e, or Kolyaycheky, ory orosh jhamanak araj lqel er lastaraqichi gorcy & ashxatowm er Shvecic och herow sghocaranowm, yndharvel er varpeti het ir՝ Kolyaycheki koghmic nerkvac cankapati spitakakarmravown gowyni hamar։ [ ] Ev orpeszi oroshaki d&ov hamozvacowtyown haghordi ir townd hayhoyanqnerin, tery cankapatic pokec erkow taxtak, meky՝ karmir, myowsy՝ spitak։ Zowt lehakan taxtaknerov kakghecrec Kolyaycheki koshowbyan tikownqy, inchi ardyownqowm arajacan xarowyki hamar pitani aynqan tasheghner, or cecvacn iren bacardakapes iravasow hamarec henc hajord parzka astghayin gishery krak gcel norakarowyc & spitakecvac sghocaran՝ i pars masnatvac Lehastani miavorman։ 
 Ayspisov, Kolyaycheky hrdig er, angam bazmahrdig, qanzi dran hajordac jhamanakahatvacowm Ar&mtyan Prowsiayi oghj taracqi sghocarannern ow pahestnery azgayin zgacmownqneri erkerangowtyan hamar orpes hrashali tasheghner ein ogtagorcvowm։ Ev, inchpes amen angam, erb xosq er linowm Lehastani apagayi masin, ayd erkow hrdehneri jhamanak el Kowys Mariamy leheri koghmn er։ Kan nowynisk akanatesner, ynd orowm omanq, hnaravor e, oghj en minch ors, ovqer mi sharq ayrvogh sghocaranneri paytamaceri vra irenc sepakan achqerov tesel en tagy glxin Astvacamory։ Isk amboxy, ory mshtapes kowtakvowm er mec hrdehneri jhamanak, ibr te bazmadayn orhnerg er ergowm i pars Astvacacni՝ Astco Mor․ sranic djhvar che entadrowtyown anel, or kolyaychekyan hrdehneri jhamanak tirowm er handisavor iravitwak, & erdowmner ein trvowm։ 
 Ev orqan canracac er ancyaly pntrvogh hrdig Kolyaycheki vra, aynqan anarat, anot&an, anvnas, poqr֊inch sahmanapak, ashxarhowm och meki koghmic choronvogh, grete bolorin ancanot er lastavar Yozef Vrankan, ory parberabar ir camelow towtowny bajhanowm er amenorya chapabajhinneri, aynqan jhamanak, qani der Bowg gety chyndownec nran ir jreri mej, isk towtowni ereq orakan bajhinnery mnacin nra batwkoni grpanowm, pastatghteri het miasin։ Qani or jrowm xeghdvac Vrankan och mi depqowm cher karogh krkin haytnvel, & och oq olor֊molor harcer cher talis nra anhetacman kapakcowtyamb, Kolyaycheky, orn owner motavorapes nowyn kazmvacqy & nmanapes kroraglowx er, inchpes & xeghdvacy, skzbowm mtav nra batwkoni mej, aynowhet&, nra pashtonakan pastatghtayin anbasir ancyalov kerpari mej, et varjhvec cxamortw cxelowc, ancav towtown camelown, pox arav nowynisk Vrankayi zowt andnakan hatkanishnery, orinak՝ artasanowtyan terowtyownnery, & hetaga bolor tarinerin nerkayacrec howsali, xnayogh, poqr֊inch kakazogh lastavari, ory Nemani, Bobii, Bowgi & Vayqseli aperic jrov loghalow er owgharkowm amboghj antarner։ Mnowm e miayn avelacnel, or ayd Vrankan Leyb֊howsar tagajharangi mot, Maqqenzineri glxavorowtyamb, carayelov hasav efreytori kochman, qani or iskakan Vrankan der carayowtyan mej cher eghel, ayn depqowm, erb Kolyaycheky, ory chors tarov aveli mec er, qan xeghdvacy, arden hascrel er iren shat vat drs&orel Torni hretanavorneri mot։ 
 Bolor avazakneri, mardaspanneri & hrdigneri aravel vtangavor masy, der koghoptely, spanely & hrdehely chdadarecrac, spasowm e, te erb hnaravorowtyown kyndervi zbaghvel aravel patvaber gorcov։ Ev shaterin nman hajoghowtyown nerkayanowm e՝ erbemn ayn, inch pntrowm ein, erbemn patahakan։ Kolyaycheky՝ darnalov Vranka, miajhamanak dardav lav & ir krake aratic ayn astitwan bowjhvac amowsin, or doghocqi er hasnowm nowynisk sovorakan lowckow tesqic։ Lowckow towpery, oronq azat ow anxrov drvac ein xohanoci seghani vra, och mi angam apahovagrvac chein nra otndgowtyownneric՝ chnayac tvowm er, te hatkapes na e yndownak lowcki horinel։ Nman gaytakghowtyowny na dowrs er netowm lowsamowtic։ Tatiks stipvac er shat janq tapel, orpeszi taq twashy jhamanakin dni seghanin։ Erbemn yntaniqy yndhanrapes nstowm er xavari mej, orovhet& kerosini lampy mnowm er aranc kraki։ 
 Ev, aynowamenayniv, Vrankan amen&in el brnapet cher։ Kiraki orery na ir Annayin tanowm er ekegheci՝ Nerqin qaghaq, ynd orowm towyl er talis nran, orpes pashtonapes nshanvac, hagnel, inchpes ayn jhamanak, kartofili dashtowm, chors shrjazgest, meky myowsi vrayic։ Dmrany, erb getery patvel ein sarowycov, & lastavarneri hamar ekel ein djhvar jhamanakner, na twshtapahoren nstowm er Troilowm, ortegh aprowm ein miayn lastavarnery, bernakirnery & navashinarani banvornery, & xnamowm er Agnes anownov aghjkan, orn aknhaytoren nman er hory, orovhet& ete asenq cher mtnowm mahtwakali tak, apa, gone hastat, bardranowm er hagowsti paharani vra, isk erb hyowrer ein galis, mtnowm er seghani tak, & nra het miasin՝ na& ir late tikniknery։ 
 Ayspisov, Agnesy sirowm er taqnvel achqeric & ayd taqstocowm iren zgowm er nowynchap howsali, orchap Yozefy, chnayac or ayntegh gtnowm er ayl owraxowtyownner, qan nranq, oronq Yozefy gtav Annayi shrjazgestneri tak։ Hrdig Kolyaycheky bavakanachap pordarow er, orpeszi haskanar taqstocneri handep ir aghjka dgtowmy, ayd isk pattwarov patshgambin poxarinogh elowsti vra, orov avartvowm er nranc mekowkes senyakanoc bnakarany, na twagarneri hamar ankyown er karowcowm։ Dra koghqin na karowcec na& bowyn՝ twisht nra hasakov։ Ayd karowycowm nstowm er im manowk mayry, xaghowm er ir tiknikneri het & mi&nowyn jhamanak mecanowm։ Hetagayowm, arden ashakertowhi, na, yst patmowtyownneri, mi koghm gcec ir tikniknerin & zvartwanalov apake howlownqnerov & xaytabghet gndiknerov, arajin angam dgtowm zgac depi pxrown gegheckowtyowny։ 
 Howsov em, or ind, or ayrvowm em sepakan kyanqi akownqnery nerkayacnelow cankowtyamb, towyl ktrvi dadarecnel Vrankayi yntaniqi nkaragrowtyowny։ Nranc amowsnakan lasty hangist sahowm e hosanqov, yndhowp minch& tasnereq tivy, erb Shixaowi motakayqowm navaranic ijav «Kolowmbosy», qani or ostikanowtyowny, ory erbeq ochinch cher moranowm, ynkav keghc Vrankayi hetqi vra։ 
 Sksvec nranic, or Kolyaycheky՝ inchpes amen amran avartin mot, aynpes el   t․ ogostosin, petq e mec lasty qsher Ki&ic՝ Pripyati vrayov, Bowgowic minch& Modlina dgvogh jrancqov & arden dranic heto՝ Vayqselov։ Tasnerkow lastanaver dowrs ekan «Radaowna» navaqarsh shogenavi vra, ory cowx er ardakowm, sksac Ar&mtyan Noyferic՝ Merac Vayqselov minch& Aynlage։ Aynowhet& Vayqselov depi ver՝ Kezemarkayi, Leckaowi, Chatkaowi, Dirshaowi & Pikelyayi koghqov & erekoyan xarisx gcec Torni apin։ Ayntegh nav bardracav nor tery, ory Ki&owm petq e het&er paytanyowti gnmany։ Erb aravotyan  ֊in «Radaownan» meknec, haytni dardav, or tery navi vra e։ Kolyaychekn arajin angam nran tesav navi arj&i masi taxtakamaci vra naxatwashelis։ Nranq nstel ein henc dem֊dimac, camowm ein & xmowm gare sowrtwy։ Kolyaycheky anmijapes twanachec nran։ Hastot, arden twaghatacac mardy kargadrec oghi berel & lcnel sowrtwi datark gavatneri mej։ Sharownakelov camel, erb taxtakamaci verjowm der lcnowm ein oghin, na nerkayacav։ 
 ― Orpeszi dowq imanaq՝ es nor tern em, ind Dyowkerhof en anvanowm, & es boloric karg ow kanon em pahanjowm։ 
 Tiroj pahanjov lastavarnery՝ ayn hajordakanowtyamb, orov nstac ein seghani dimac, haytnowm ein irenc anownnery & koncowm gavatnery aynpes, or adamaxndornery ver֊ver ein trchowm։ Isk Kolyaycheky nax koncec, heto asac «Vranka», inchpes krknowm er myows lastavarneri anownnery։ Ev, aynowhanderd, Kolyaychekin tvac, te Dyowkerhofy arandnacrec xeghdvac lastavari anowny och te ktrowk, ayl aveli showt mtaxoh։ 
 Mimyanc hertapoxogh navatarneri ognowtyamb, arhestavarjhoren xowsapelov avazot cancaghowtneric, «Radaownan» haghtaharowm er pghtor, kavot shity, ory miayn mi owghghowtyown giter։ Aj ow dax derqi owghghowtyamb hoghatmberic ayn koghm ynkac er hart kam poqr֊inch tmbavorvac hoghy, ori vrayic arden havaqel ein berqy։ Kendani cankapatnery, doraknery, orotwov cackvac gogahovity & gyowghakneri mij& ynkac hartavayry, ory karces steghcvac e hecelazori hardakowmneri hamar։ Daxic avazov li arkgher ein drvac՝ owlanakan diviziayi hamar, cankapati vrayov trchogh howsarneri hamar, eritasard rotmaystrneri eraghanqneri hamar, menamarti hamar։ Aystegh ein tambakeri mot ekac tatarnery, dragownnery, erazkot aspetnery՝ arshavelow yntacqowm ynknogh, & ordeni magistrosnery՝ gownavor tiknocnerov։ Lanjapanaki vrayi bolor twarmandnery anvnas ein, baci miakic՝ ory ktrel e dowqs Mazaveckin, & diery, ― och mi krkesowm nman arabakan njhowygner ches tesni, ― nyardayin, hoyakap dastapanacoperi tak, bolor nyardery dgvac, inchpes qanonov, rowngery owrac, bosoragowyn՝ drancic dowrs en galis ampikner, nizaknerov xocvac։ Nizaknery ijecvac en & bajhanowm en erkinqy, erekoyi verjalowysy, na& trer, isk ayntegh, etin planowm, ― qani or yowraqanchyowr nkar owni ir etin plany, ― amowr parvelov horizonin, xaghagh «ayrvowm e» gyowghaky, diow et&i otqeri aranqowm mamowrov patvac kartwlik hyowghakner՝ cghotov cackvac։ Isk hyowghakneri mej՝ tanker, geghecik, konservacvac, apaga oreri spasman mej, erb irenc &s towyl ktan haytnvel ays ktavi vra, ays hartavayrowm՝ Vayqseli hoghapatneshneric ayn koghm, inchpes tet&otn zambiknerin՝ hecelazori mej։ 
 Vlaclaveki mot Dyowkerhofy matov bzec Kolyaychekin․ «Isk asaceq ind, Vranka, dowq patahabar, tariner araj Shveci sghocaranowm che՞q ashxatel։ Ayn jhamanak ayrvec sghocarany, che՞»։ 
 Kolyaycheky hamaroren, karces dimadrowtyowny haghtaharelov, glowxy tap tvec & nran hajoghvec ir achqerin tal hognac & vshtabek artahaytowtyown, aynpes, or Dyowkerhofy, ori vra ynkav ayd hayacqy, dernpah mnac hataga harcowporderic։ 
 Erb Modlini tak՝ ayntegh, ortegh Bowgy tapvowm e Vayqseli mej, «Radaownan» shrjvec, Kolyaycheky՝ araj teqvac, ereq angam tqec, inchpes da yndownvac e bolor lastanaveri mot, koghqin haytnvec Dyowkerhofy ir sigarov & nranic krak xndrec։ Ayd bary, «lowcki» bari pes, xocec Kolyaychekin։ «Ayd incho՞w eq dowq karmrowm, erb es krak em xndrowm։ Aghjik e՞q, inch e»։ 
 Nranq hascrel ein Modliny toghnel shat et, erb Kolyaycheki eresic i verjo ijav nerky, orn amen&in el amotxacowtyan nerk cher, ayl՝ ir koghmic ayrac sghocaranneri owshacac colq։ 
 Modlini & Ki&i mij&, kartw asac՝ Bowgov depi ver, jrancqi mijov, ory miacnowm e Bowgy Pripyatin, teghi chownecav ochinch, inchy kareli er hamarel Vrankayi & Dyowkerhofi mij& banakcowtyownner։ Hatwax navaqarsh shogenavi vra lastanaveri mij&, hnocapanneri & lastavarneri mij&, ghekapeteri ow navapeti mij&, navapeti ow mshtapes popoxvogh navatarneri mij& inch֊or ban teghi er ownenowm, inchpes & petq e liner, isk hnaravor e, inchpes & linowm e tghamardkanc mij&։ Es kkaroghanayi patkerel anhashtowtyownnery kashowbyan lastavarneri & navatari mij&, ory cnowndov Shtetinic er։ Hnaravor e՝ kayin nowynisk xrovowtyan saghmer՝ yndhanowr havaqner taxtakamaci dax koghmowm։ Nranq vitwakahanowtyown en anowm, nshanaban en horinowm, danakner en srowm։ 
 Sakayn chxosenq ayd masin։ Teghi chownecan o՛ch qaghaqakan gorcoghowtyownner, o՛ch leh֊germanakan danakaharowtyownner, o՛ch tvyal xmbin hamapatasxanogh, socialakan anardarowtyamb cnvac xrovowtyown։ Barextworen xjhrelov qaracowxy՝ «Radaownan» gnowm er ir owghiov, mi angam, im hishelov da anmijapes Ploky ancnelowc heto er, ayn nstec avazot cancaghowti vra, sakayn karoghacav sepakan owjherov azatvel։ Kartw, townot replikneri poxanakowm noyfarvaserci navapet Barbowshi ow owkrainaci navastow mij&՝ aha & amboghjy։ Nowynisk navamatyany cher karogh or&e ban avelacnel։ 
 Sakayn ete es ownenayi Kolyaycheki mtqery kam dyowkerhofyan sghocaranneri kyanqi jhamanakagrowtyowny navamatyanowm grancelow partakanowtyown & cankowtyown, dranowm bavakanachap kxosver popoxowtyownneri & arkacneri, kaskacanqneri & hastatowmneri, anvastahowtyan masin &, grete anmijapes, ayd anvstahowtyan showtapowyt veracman masin։ Vaxenaly՝ erkowsn el ein vaxenowm, isk Dyowkerhofy՝ nowynisk aravel, qan Kolyaycheky, qani or nranq gtnvowm ein Rowsastanowm, & Dyowkerhofy heshtowtyamb karogh er dowrs ynknel navic, inchpes jhamanakner araj xeghtw Vrankan։ Minch ayd arden Ki&owm enq՝ paytanyowti vatwarqi pahestneric mekowm, oronq aynqan mec en ow antesaneli, or ayd xarnashpotowtyan mej liovin kareli e korcnel sepakan pahapan hreshtakin, ynknel hankarcaki sharjhowm sksac geranneri darsakowyti tak, & da ayl&s ches kasecni։ Ax, orqan lav kliner, ete ays teghowm es karoghnayi teghekacnel, te inchpes e kisaxeghdvac & kam grete twzmvac Dyowkerhofy՝ der canr shnchelov & hayacqowm mahvan nshannerov, keghc Vrankayi akanjin shshnjowm․ «Shnorhakalowtyown, Kolyaychek, shnorhakalowtyown» &, anhrajhesht dadaric heto, «Ayjhm es ow dow mer hashivnery pakel enq & morananq amen inchi masin»։ 
 Ev nranq, orpes townd ynkerner, shpotvac jhptalov, grete arcownqot achqerov knayein mimyanc, inchpes tghamardik en nayowm, & kpoxanakvein erkchot, sakayn koshtowkot, derqseghmowmnerov։ 
 Ays tesarany mez hrashali canot e gitakcowtyan mtagnecman astitwan varpetowtyamb nkarahanvac filmeric, erb hankarc rejhisori glxowm apshecowcich mitq e cagowm՝ derasanowtyownner anogh eghbayr֊tshnaminerin veracel ynker֊hamaxohneri, oronq der petq e hamategh ancnen kraki ow jri, hazaravor arkacneri mijov։ 
 Sakayn Kolyaychekin aydpes el chvitwakvec o՛ch toghnel, or Dyowkerhofy gna depi hataky, o՛ch el՝ glorvogh geranneri tak ynknelow & mahvan twiranneric hanelow hnaravorowtyown։ Harazat dernarkowtyan shahi masin mtacelov՝ Dyowkerhofy Ki&owm gnec antari xmbaqanaky, owshadir het&ec, te inchpes en hyowsowm & jowrn ijecnowm iny lastery, &, sovorowtyan hamadayn, lastavarneri mij& manr caxseri hamar bajhanec patkareli qanakowtyamb rowsakan dramner, inchic heto nstec gnacq, ory nran Varshava֊Modlin֊Doych֊Eylaow֊Marienbowrg֊Dirshaow ertowghov hascrec dernarkowtyown, ori sghocarannery teghakayvac ein Klaviteri & Shixaowi navashinararneri mij& ynkac paytanyowti navamatowycneri erkaynqov։ 
 Naxqan lastavarnerin՝ mi qani shabatya lrjagowyn ashxatanqic heto bolor geteri, jrancqneri &, i verjo, Vayqseli mijov ancnelow hnaravorowtyown ynderely, es ind harc em talis․ hastat hamozva՞c er, ardoyq, Dyowkerhofy, or Vrankan henc hrdig Kolyaychekn e։ Ev owzowm em asel, or minch sghocarani tery navarkowm er anvnas, barehogi & bolori koghmic sirvac Vrankayi het, howys owner, or ir twanaparhakicy Kolyaycheky che, orn ownak e katarel or&e handowgn qayl։ Ayd howysic na hrajharvec, miayn erb nstac er vagoni xciki barderi vra։ Sakayn minch& gnacqy hasav minch& verjin kayarany՝ mtnelov Dancig qaghaqi kentronakan kayarani kamarneri tak, ayjhm es i verjo artaberowm em ayd anvanowmy, Dyowkerhofy ekav ir dyowkerhofyan ezrakacowtyownnerin, hramayec ir twamprowknery teghapoxel karq, isk karqin՝ gnal town, isk andamb inqy arowyg, arden aranc owgheberi, slacav depi motaka ostikanankan naxagahowtyown, Vibenvalshtrase, ayntegh՝ astitwannerov trchkotelov hasav glxavor shqamowtqin։ Kartwat&, sakayn manrakrkit oronowmneric heto na gtav ayn senyaky, ortegh chapic aveli gorcarar mtnolort er tirowm, orpeszi lsein Dyowkerhofi kartw, miayn pastery nerkayacnogh hashvetvowtyowny։ Dranic chi het&owm, te sghocarani tery haytararowtyown arec։ Och, na owghghaki xndrec zbaghvel Kolyaychek֊Vrankayi gorcov, inchy & xostacan anel ostikannery։ 
 Verjin shabatneri yntacqowm, minch gnvac paytamterqic patrastvac lastery eghegni holikneri & lastavarneri het dandagh sahowm ein getn i var, bazmativ varchowtyownner bazmativ tghter ein kazmowm։ Vercnenq, orinak, Yozef Kolyaycheki՝ ar&mtaprowsakan gndi dashtayin hretanow aysinch hamari sharqayin hretanavori zinvorakan gorcy։ Ankarg hretanavory ereq ory erkow angam masnaki kalanqi tak e gtnvel alkoholayin harbacowtyan, inchpes na& kisagermaneren, kisaleheren orotadayn anarxistakan lozowngner goralow hamar։ Mi xosqov, anpativ bcer, oronq chhajoghvec haytnaberel efreytor Vrankayi tghterowm, ory carayel er Langfowri erkrord layb֊howsarakan gndowm։ Hakaraky, efreytor Vrankan iren drs&orel er lav koghmov, taktikakan parapmownqneri jhamanak hatweli tpavorowtyown er toghel tagajharangi vra & verjinics stacel er ayd aritneri hamar grpanowm pahvogh taler՝ tagajharangi taler։ Sakayn ayd talery ardanagrvac cher efreytor Vrankayi zinvorakan tghterowm, inchi masin bardr lac ow kocov teghekacrec im Anna taty, erb harcaqnnowm ein nran & nra Vincent anownov eghbory։ 
 Sakayn im taty miayn ayd taleri ognowtyamb che, or twakatamart er mghowm ynddem «hrdig» bari։ Och, na karogh er nerkayacnel pastatghter, oronq bazmaki angam hastatowm ein, or Yozef Vrankan arden  t․ er inqnakam dardel Dancig֊Nidershtadti hrjej drowjhinayi andam & dmerayin amisnerin, erb lastavarneri hamar merac shrjan e, payqarel e bazmativ mec ow poqr hrdehneri dem։ Ayd tghteri mej kar na& patvogir, ory vkayowm er, or hrshej Vrankan Troili erkatowghayin mec depoyowm   t․ och te parzapes hrdehner er hangcnowm, ayl krakic prkel e pakanagorci erkow ashakertnerin։ Twisht nowyn kerp artahaytvec na& orpes vka hravirvac brandmayster Hexty։ Ardanagrowtyan hamar na haytnec het&yaly․ 
 ― Inchpe՞s karogh e hrdig linel na, or inqn e hrdeh hangcnowm։ Axr, es minch ors el tesnowm em, te inchpes er na kangnac hrshej astitwani vra, erb ayrvowm er Hoybowdi ekeghecin։ Pyownik, ory harnowm e moxric ow krakic & hangcnowm och miayn kraky, ayl& ays ashxarhi hrdehy & mer Tiroj, Hisows Qristosi caravy։ Twshmarit em asowm es dez, lav e jraghaci qar kaxel ayn mardow vzic, or hrdig makanownn e talis ays hrashali Pyowniqin, hrsheji saghavartov mardown, orn ogtvowm e ert&ekelow aravelowtyan iravownqic, orin sirowm en apahovagrakan gorcakalowtyownnery, ory misht ir grpanowm e krowm mi bowr moxir՝ orpes xorhrdanish kam masnagitowtyan nshan։ 
 Dowq, havanabar, arden nkateciq, or brandmayster Hexty՝ kamavor hrshej drowjhinayi kapitany, twartaraxos hog&orakan er․ na kiraki orery kangnowm er Langgarteni Sowrb Barbara cxakan ekeghecow ambioni arj& &, qani der datavarowtyown er yntanowm ynddem Kolyaychek֊Vrankayi, arity bac cher toghnowm nmanatip artahaytowtyownnerov ir hoti glowxy lcnel erknayin hrsheji & djhoxqi hrdigi masin araknerov։ 
 Sakayn qani or qreakan ostikanowtyan pashtonyannery Sowrb Barbarayi ekeghecin chein hatwaxowm &, dran gowmarac, «Pyowni q» bari mej aveli showt norin Tagavorakan mecowtyan handep viravoranq ein ditowm, verjinis gorcowneowtyowny inqnakam drowjhinayowm ynkalowm ein orpes canracowcich hangamanq։ 
 Havaqowm ein tarber sghocaranneric cowcmownqner, teghi hamaynqneric vkayowtyownner․ Vrankan lowys ashxarh er ekel Towxelowm, minch Kolyaycheky cnowndov Tornic er։ Mi sharq poqrik anhamapatasxanowtyownner mecahasak lastavarneri & nranc heravor azgakanneri cowcmownqnerowm։ Kowjhy misht dgtowm e depi jowry, & nran owrish ochinch chi mnowm, qan kotrvel։ Qani der harcaqnnowtyownnery yntanowm ein irenc hownov, lasteri qaravany motenowm er petakan sahmanin &, Tornic sksac, gtnvowm er gaghtni hskoghowtyan tak, isk kangarnerowm aravel &s։ 
 Papiks ayd nkatec miayn Dirshaowic heto, qani or dran na spasowm er։ Sakayn ayd jhamanak nran tirac pasivowtyowny, ory sahmanakcowm er melanxoliayi het, havanabar towyl chtvec nran paxowsti pord dernarkel depi Leckaow kam Kezemark։ Da miangamayn karogh er psakvel hajoghowtyamb՝ ayd vayrerowm nran shatery twanachowm ein, & lastavarnery hamakranq ein tacowm nra nkatmamb։ Aynlageic sksac, erb lastery dandagh, meky myowsin hrelov, mtnowm ein Merac Vayqsel, mi inch֊or dknorsakan motoranavak annkat slacav motikic, bayc nkatvec, or ayntegh chapic dowrs mecativ andnakazm kar։ Plenendorfic anmijapes heto eghegnowtneric ashxowyjh dowrs tran navahangsti ostikanowtyan zowyg motorabarkasnery & sksecin laynqov ow erkaynqov tweghqel Merac Vayqseli jrery, oronq irenc nexahotov aveli ow aveli ein vkayowm navahangsti motikowtyan masin։ Isk Hoybowdin hajordac kamrji ayn koghmowm arden sksvowm er «kapowyt hamazgestneri» argelapakocayin shghtan։ Klavitetyan navashinarani dimaci antaranyowti darsaknery, poqrik navakayin navashinarannery, Motlaowi owghghowtyamb gnalov aveli laynacogh antaranyowti navahangistnery, amenatarber sghocaranneri navamatowycayin kamrjaknery, sepakan dernarkowtyan kamrjaky՝ ays ameni showrjbolory kayin «kapowyt hamazgestavorner»։ Nranq kayin amenowr, miayn Shirxaowi mot nranq chkayin․ ayntegh amen inch zardarvac er droshaknerov, & teghi er ownenowm inch֊or ayl gorcoghowtyown, ankaskac inch֊or meky piti ijner navasandowghqov։ Ayntegh bavakan shat mardik ein havaqvel, inchn anhangstacnowm er twayerin, ayntegh ton er nshvowm՝ ardo՞q och im papiki patvin։ 
 Miayn erb im papiky tesav paytanyowteri navamatowycnerowm kowtakvac «kapowytnerin», & erb e՛l aveli charaghet sksec er&al barkasneri koghmic yntrac ertowghin, oroncic taracvogh aliqnery arden mtrakowm ein lasterin, na haskacav, or bolor owjheri ays kowtakowmy kapvac er ir het։ Nra mej artnacav hrdig Kolyaycheki sirty, na irenic bajhanec anchar Vrankayin, inqnakam dowrs ekav hrshej drowjhinayi kazmic, oghj daynov & aranc tatanvelow hrajharvec kakazogh Vrankayic & vazec lasteri vrayov, laynardak ererown hartowtyownneri vrayov։ Otabobik vazec chrandac «manrahataki» vrayov, mi geranic depi myowsy՝ Shixaowi owghghowtyamb, ortegh qamow dimac owrax droshner ein cacanvowm։ Na vazec araj taxtakneri vrayov, ayntegh, owr navaranneri vra inch֊or ban er drvac, ortegh geghecik elowytner ein ownenowm, ortegh och oq dayn cher talis Vrankayin, isk aravel &s Kolyaychekin, ortegh asowm ein ayspes․ «Es anvanowm em qez anownov՝ Norin Mecowtyan navatormi «Kolowmbos» nav, Amerika, aveli qan qarasown hazar tonna jrataroghowtyamb, eresown hazar diaowjh»։ Norin Mecowtyan navatormi nav, arajin kargi cxelow srah, navaxeli vra erkrord kargi xohanoc, marmaric sportayin dahlitw, gradaran, Amerika, Norin Mecowtyan navatormi nav, tiavarogh liseri mijancq, zbosanqayin taxtakamac՝ parqi haghtakan dapniov, harazat navamatowyci tonakan drosh, arqayazn Haynrixy kangnac e gheki mot, isk im Kolyaychek papiky՝ otabobik, otqerov haziv gerannerin dipchelov, poghayin erajhshtowtyany yndaraj։ Jhoghovowrd, orn ayspisi ishxanner owni, oronq, navarkelov, irenc showrjy՝ mshtakan tonaxmbowtyownnerov, parqi haghtakan dapniov, navahangstowm karanac bolor naveri shchaknerov mardkanc ein havaqowm։ Navaqarsh shogenaver & shogenaver zvartwali zbosanqneri hamar, Kolowmbos, Amerika, azatowtyown & erkow barkas՝ owraxowtyownic xelqnery trcrac․ bolory nra et&ic, mi lastic depi myowsy։ Norin Mecowtyan lastery pakowm en twanaparhy & pchacnowm xaghy, aynpes, or na petq e kang arni, minchder aynqan lav tap er havaqel, & na men֊miaynak kangnac e lasti vra & tesnowm e arden Amerikan, isk barkasnery mtnowm en layn koghmic․ de inch, petq e et hrvel՝ aha arden im papy loghowm e, loghowm depi lasty, ory mtnowm e Motlaow։ Isk ayjhm stipvac e sowzvel & mnal jri tak barkasneri pattwarov, isk lasty sharjhvec nra vra, & ayd lastin verj chkar․ eli nor laster․ last qo lastic & havitayns havitenic last։ 
 Barkasnery anjatecin sharjhichnery, & anoghoq zowyg achqery sksecin znnel jri maker&owyty։ Aakayn Kolyaycheky hrajhesht er tvel mekyndmisht, heracel er shchakneri tetghya ornocic, navayin zangakneric, Norin Mecowtyan navatormi navic & knownqi kapakcowtyamb elowytic, orn artasanec arqayazn Haynrixy, Norin Mecowtyan xelakorowys twayeric, parqi haghtakan dapnowc, Norin Mecowtyan navatormi navi navasandowghqi aravel sahownowtyan hamar Norin Mecowtyan heghowk otwaric, Amerikayic, «Kolowmbosic» & na& ostikanakan hetaqnnowtyownneric՝ haverjh heracav verj chownecogh lasti tak։ 
 Im papi marminy aydpes el erbeq chhaytnabervec։ Es hastat hamozvac em nranowm, or na ir mahy gtav lasteri tak, petq e, sakayn, chsasandem asvaci handep vstahowtyowny, ind vra canrowtyown vercnem & sharadrem hrashali prkowtyownneri bolor tarberaknery։ Ayspisov, mardik patmowm ein, or nran hajoghvel e lasti tak, geranneri aranqowm tweghq haytnaberel, nerq&ic bavakanachap layn, orpeszi qitn ow berany pahi jric dowrs, isk depi ver ayd tweghqy aynqan er neghanowm, or antesaneli er mnowm ostikanneri hamar, oronq minch& owsh gisher xowzarkowm ein lastery & nowynisk nranc vrayi eghege holiknery։ Aynowhet& mtowtyan qoghi tak, aydpes er asvowm, paps trvec aliqneri kamqin &, chnayac korcrel er owjhery, baxti oroshaki berowmov hasav Shixaowi navashinarani taracqi՝ Motlaowi hakarak apy, ayntegh taqnvec taponneri sari mej, isk aveli owsh, hnaravor e howyn navastineri ognowtyamb, haytnvec ayn keghtot bernatar naveric meki vra, oronq yst asekosneri, mek paxstakani che, or apastan ein tvel։ 
 Owrishnery xosowm en ayspes․ Kolyaycheky na& loghord er, isk nra toqery aravel lavn ein, & na loghac ancav och miayn lasti takov, och, na jri takov ancav na& mnacac, Motlaowi bavakanin layn masy, barehajogh ap hasac Shirxaowi navashinarani taracqowm, ayntegh, or ir vra owshadrowtyown chgravelov, xarnvec banvorneri xmbin, isk aveli owsh՝ na& cncacogh mardkanc & jhoghovrdi het mektegh ergec «Parq qez՝ haghtanakac dapniov», Norin Mecowtyan navatormi «Kolowmbia» navn ocelow jhamanak arqayazn Haynrixi elowytic heto, capaharec՝ navy navaranic barehajogh jowrn ijecnelowc heto & amboxi het miasin՝ kisov chap choracac hagowstov lqec tonaxmbowtyowny & arden hatord ory, ― asytegh arajin varkacy mianowm e erkrordin, ― orpes anvtwar owgh&or՝ na bardracav hrchak derq berac hownakan bernanav։ 
 Patkeri amboghjakanowtyan hamar hark e verhishel na& errord animast varkacy, hamadayn ori՝ im papy՝ orpes logharkvogh antaranyowt, dowrs bervec bac cov, ortegh nran anhapagh orsacin Bonzaki dknorsnery &, ereq milionanoc gotow sahmanneric dowrs, poxancecin ovkianosayin navagnacowtyany harmarecvac shvedakan motoranavakin։ Varkacy hrashali d&ov towyl er talis, or shvedakan motoranavaki vra na dandagh verakangner owjhery & hasner minch& Malmye kam nman or&e mi tegh։ 
 Ays ameny anhetetowtyown e & dknorsakan pchocner։ Twisht nowyn kerp es och mi arjheq chem talis bacardakapes navahangstayin qaghaqneri akanatesneri anarjhanahavat tarber patmowtyownnerin, ovqer ibr im papin tesel en Arajin hamashxarhayin paterazmi avartic qich anc Bowfaloyowm (AMN)։ Nran karces anvanowm ein Jo Kolchik, & or na, yst patmoghneri xosqeri, zbaghvac er Kanadayi het antaranyowti ar&trov։ Lowckow dernarkowtyownneri bajhnetomser։ Apahovagrakan gorcakalowtyan himnadir՝ apahovagrowm e hrdehic։ Nran nkaragrowm ein orpes chapic dowrs harowst mi mardow․ ibr na nstac er erknaqeri hskayakan graseghani mot, bolor matnerin՝ paylogh qarerov mataniner, zinavarjhanq e anckacnowm ir tiknapahneri het, oronq krowm en hrsheji hamazgest, karoghanowm en ergel leheren & anvanvowm en Pyowniki Gvardia։ 
 «Titerniky & lampy» 
 Mi mard toghec ir ownecac amen inchy, ancav ovkianosy, hasav Amerika & harstacav՝ sranov es kamenowm em avartel im papi masin bolor xosakcowtyownnery, inchpes el or na iren anvaner․ leheren՝ Golyachek, kashowbyan d&ov՝ Kolyaychek kam amerikyan d&ov՝ Jo Kolchik։ 
 Bavakan bard e titeghya tmbowki shnorhiv, orpisiq vatwarowm en xaghaliqneri xanowtnerowm & hanraxanowtnerowm, tmbkaharelov ver hanel payti՝ grete horizoni ayn koghm heracogh lastery։ Ev, aynowhanderd, ind hajoghvec tmbkaharel paytanyowti navahangisty, oghj jraber payty, ory geti olorannerowm ororvowm e jri vra, qrqrvowm e eghegnowtnerowm, poqr֊inch aveli heshtowtyamb ind hajoghvec tmbkaharel shixaowyan & klaviteryan navashinararneri angarnery, bazmativ՝ mec masamb navakneri manr veranorogmamb zbaghvogh, navashinarannery, vagonashinakan gorcaranin kic metaghakan jardoni kowyty, margarini fabrikayin kic darnaham kokosneri pahestnery, Shpayxer kghzow՝ ind haytni bolor etnaxorshery։ Paps mahacav, na ind patasxan chi ta, hetaqrqrowtyown chi drs&ori navashinaranic jowrn ijecrac kayzerakan navi handep, erbemn tasnamyakner dgdgvogh, sakayn jowrn ijnelow pahic sksac mahvann yndaraj yntacogh, orin mer depqowm tvel ein «Kolowmbos» anvanowmy, anvanowm ein na& navatormi hpartowtyown։ Ayn, bnakanoren, owghghowtyown vercrec depi Amerika, isk aveli owsh kam xortakecin, kam inqy xortakvec։ Hnaravor e, or ayn ver hanecin hatakic, verapoxecin, veranvanecin kam ogtagorcecin orpes jardon։ Hnaravor e na&, or «Kolowmbosy» owghghaki heracav jri hatak, inchpes jhamanakin varvec im papy, gowce na minch aysor hosyntac tarvowm e ir oghj qarasown hazaranoc jratarowtyamb, cxelow hamar naxatesvac srahov, marmarya sportayin dahlitwov, loghavazanov & mersman arandnasenyaknerov, xorqowm e, asenq   m, inch֊or tegh filippinyan ijvacqowm kam Emendi owghghowtyamb․ dra masin kareli e yntercel «Veyerowm» kam covayin oracowycnerowm՝ hishowm em, och ayn e arajin, och ayn e erkrord «Kolowmbosy» inqnakam ijav hatak, orovhet& navapety chkaroghacav tanel paterazmi het kapvac mi inch֊or xaytarakowtyown։ 
 Lastayin patmowtyan mi masy es bardradayn kardaci Brownoyin, oric heto tveci im harcy՝ pndelov, or patasxany lini obyektiv։ 
 ― Hrashali mah, ― erazkotowtyamb artasanec Brownon & anmijapes sksec kapel xeghdvac papis ir yndownvac lar֊kaperov։ Es stipvac ei bavararvel nman patasxanov & im mtqeri handowgn trichqy chowghghel depi Amerika, orpeszi charcharanqov darnayi jharangowtyan ter։ Ind ayci ekan Vitlar & Klep anownov ynkerners։ Klepy berec daynaskavarak, ori erkow koghmerowm el Qing Olivern er, isk Vitlary kotratvelov ind meknec shokolade sirt՝ vardagowyn jhapaveni vra։ Nranq tarber himarowtyownner ein anowm, caghranmanakowm ein tesaranner im datavarowtyownic։ Isk es nranc hatwowyq pattwarelow hamar patkerowm ei, te inchpes en bolor aycelowtyan orerin maqrowtyown anowm, hrashali tramadrowtyown ei cowcaberowm & nowynisk՝ amenahimar katakneri vra cicaghelow ownakowtyown։ Annkat d&ov, naxqan Klepy khascner sksel ir dasaxosowtyowny jazi & marqsizmi poxadard kaperi masin, es nerkayacreci im patmowtyowny mi mardow masin, ory tasnereq tvin, och shat araj ayn jhamanakic, erb ayd ameny brnkvec, ynkav mi ansahman, kareli e asel, iroq, verj chownecogh lasti tak & ayl&s dowrs chprcav nra takic, nowynisk nra marminy aydpes el chgtnvec։ I patasxan im ayn harcin, ory tveci anbrnazbosik, karces te dandrali tonov՝ Klepy thatwowtyamb sharjhec hast vzi vra gtnvogh glowxy, ardakec bolor kotwaknery, heto krkin kotwkec, loghordi mi qani sharjhowmner arec՝ mi xosqov iren pahec aynpes, karces henc inqn er gtnvowm lasti tak։ Verji i verjo na xowsapec im harcic՝ patasxani bacakayowtyan hamar meghqy gcelov chapazanc vagh mpnshaghi vra։ 
 Vitlary nstac er lowr, otqy otqi vra gcac & mi&nowyn jhamanak chmoranalov shalvari calqeri masin, nstel & cowcadrowm er ayn nrbatwashak, gcavor, artasovor inqnahavanowtyowny, ory hatowk e ter&s miayn erknayin hreshtaknerin։ 
 ― Es gtnvowm em lasti vra։ Lasti vra gtnvely hrashali e։ Ind kcowm en mocaknery։ Da thatw e։ Es gtnvowm em lasti tak։ Lasti tak hrashali e։ Mocaknery ayl&s ind chen kcowm։ Da hatweli e։ Karcowm em, or miangamayn hnaravor e aprel lasti tak, ete, iharke, dow mtadrowtyown chownes miajhamanak gtnvel na& lasti vra & towyl tal, or mocaknery qez kcen։ 
 Henc aydtegh Vitlarn arec ir pordvac dadary & owshadir nayec ind, heto, inchpes amen angam, erb owzowm er nmanvel bvi, bardracrec ir aranc ayn el bardr honqery & derasanakan artasanowtyamb artaberec․ 
 ― Ind tvowm e, or ayd xeghdvaci het kapvac, lasteri tak haytnvac mardow depqowm, xosqy qo azgakani & kam qo harazat papi masin e։ Qani or na, linelov qo azgakany, kam aravel &s՝ qo harazat papy, gitakcowm er ir partakanowtyownnery qo handep, & na henc gtav ir mahy, qanzi ashxarhowm och mi ban qez hamar aynqan tanjalic linel cher karogh, qan papid kendani linely։ Ayspisov, dow och te parzapes spanoghn es qo azgakani, ayl dran avelacrac na& spanoghn es qo harazat papi։ Sakayn, qani or verjins, isk da yndhanrapes yndownvac e papikneri mot, kcankanar qez patjhel, zrkec qez ayn hatwowyqic, orn aprowm e tory՝ hpartoren matnacowyc anelov jri mej owrac diaky & aselov het&yal xosqery․ «Nayeq im merac papin։ Na heros e eghel։ Na jowry netvec, erb tesav, or iren hetapndowm en»։ Qo papn ashxarhin & ir torany zrkec ir marminy sepakan achqerov tesnelow hnaravorowtyownic, ori miak npatakn er՝ stipel mnacoghnerin, ayd tvowm na& torany, der erkar zbaghvel irenov։ 
 Aynowhet&, mi xandavarowtyownic mowsin ancnelov, xoramank, poqr֊inch araj teqvac & hashtowtyan kniqy demqin՝ Vitlarn asac․ 
 ― Amerika։ Owraxaci՛r, Oskar։ Dow ownes npatak & ownes xndir։ Aystegh qez bnakanabar kardaracnen & bac ktoghnen։ El o՞wr gnas, ete och Amerika, ortegh krkin kareli e gtnel ameny, nowynisk korac papin։ 
 Orqan el xaytogh ow viravorakan er Vitlari patasxany, na im mej aveli mec vstahowtyown sermanec, qan kyanqi ow mahvan mij& tarberowtyowny grete chbajhanogh im ynkeroj՝ Klepi datarkaxosowtyowny kam hivandapah Brownoyi patasxany, orn im papi mahy hrashali anvanec miayn ayn pattwarov, or dranic anmijapes heto, bacelov aliqnery, navashinaranic ijav «NMN Kolowmbosy»։ Ayd isk pattwarov es parabanmamb em hatowcowm vitlaryan Amerikayin, ory pahacoyacnowm e paperin naxatesvac nshanakety, nmowshy։ Erb es, dandracac Evropayic, cankanowm em mi koghm dnel tmbowks ow grichs, asaci inqs ind․ «Sharownakir grel, Oskar, ara da hanown qo chlsvac harstowtyan ter, sakayn hognac Kolyaychek papi, ory Bowfaloyowm zbaghvac e paytanyowteri vatwarqov, isk ir erknaqeri ynderqnerowm xaghowm e lowckineri het»։ 
 Erb Klepy & Vitlary i verjo hajoghowtyown maghtecin & heracan, Brownon vtwrakanoren odapoxelov, senyakic heracrec im ynkerneri kpchown hoty։ Dranic heto es krkin vercreci im tmbowky, sakayn skseci tmbkaharel och te mahy cackogh lasteri gerannery, ayl ayn arag, trvran ritmy, orin petq e entarkvein bolor mardik   tvi ogostosic heto։ Ayd isk pattwarov im teqsty yndhowp minch& im cnndyan jhamy, karogh e miayn yndhanowr gcerov owrvagcel sgo tapori owghin, orn im papy toghec Evropayowm։ 
 Erb Kolyaychekn anhetacav lasteri tak, nranc mijic, sghocarani xarsxakayanneri kamrjakneri vra spasowm ein anhangstacac im tatiky՝ ir Agnes aghjka het, Vincent Bronskin & nra tasnyotamya ordi Yany։ Mi poqr ayn koghm kangnac er ir avag eghbayr Yozef Gregor Kolyaycheky, orin harcaqnnowtyownneri hamar kanchel ein qaghaq։ Gregory ostikanowtyany anpopox talis er mek & mi&nowyn patasxany․ 
 ― Es im eghbory grete chem el twanachowm։ Twishtn asac, gitem miayn, or nran Yozef en anvanowm, isk erb es nran tesa verjin angam, na mot tasy kam asenq tasnerkow tarekan er։ Na maqrowm er im twtqavor koshiknery & vazowm garejowr berelow, erb menq mors het garejowr einq owzowm։ 
 Chnayac miajhamanak parzvec, or im naxataty sirel e garejowr՝ ostikanowtyany nman patasxany ogowt cher talis։ Dra poxaren avag Kolyaycheki nerkayowtyownic ogowt owner im Anna tatiky։ Gregory, ory erkar tariner aprel er Shtetinowm, Berlinowm, aynowhet& Shnaydemyowlowm, ayjhm bnakowtyown er hastatel Dancigowm, ashxatanq er gtel «Twagar» amroci varodi aghacowm & erb lracav sgo՝ yndownvac mek tarin, & bolor bardowtyownnery orinak, keghc֊Vrankayi het amowsnanalow patmowtyowny, hartvel ein, parzabanvel & handnvel arxiv, amowsnacav im tatiki het, ory cher cankanowm bajhanvel Kolyaychekneric & ete och erbeq, apa, cayrahegh depqowm, aydqan arag cher amowsnana Gregori het, ete na Kolyaychek chliner։ Varodi aghacowm ashxatanqy Gregorin azatowm er xaytabghet, isk vrayic anmijapes moxragowyn hagnelow anhrajheshtowtyownic։ Nranq ereqov bnakvowm ein eli ayd nowyn mek&kes senyakanoc bnakaranowm, ory erkar tariner apastan er handisanowm hrdigi hamar։ Sakayn showtov parzvec, or bolor Kolyaycheknery irar nman chen, qanzi cher ancel mek tari, inch nranq amowsnacel ein, isk im tatikn arden stipvac er vardakalel Troili ekamtayin tneric meki nkowghy։ Vatwarelov amen kargi manrowq՝ sksac angliakan qorocic, verjacrac kaghambi koghbov՝ poqr֊inch pogh er et gcowm, orovhet& Gregory, chnayac or mi kowyt pogh er stanowm ir aghacowm, town cher berowm nowynisk amenaanhrajheshty, isk poghery caxsowm er harbecoghowtyan vra։ Gregory, ory er&i im naxatatin er nmanvel, harbecogh er, minchder im Yozef papy hazvadep hatwowyqov xmowm er miayn mi bajhak։ Gregory vat tramadrowtyownic er, or xmowm er։ Nowynisk ayn jhamanak, erb nra mot, tvowm er, te lav tramadrowtyown e, isk da hatwax cher patahowm, qani or na hakowm owner depi melanxolian, na xmowm er och te owraxanalow hamar, ayl ayn pattwarov, or cankanowm er hasnel yowraqanchyowr ararkayi eowtayny, ayd tvowm՝ na& alkoholi eowtyany։ Qani der Gregory oghj er, och meky och mi angam chi tesel, or na gihii trmoghow bajhaky kisxmel toghner։ 
 Mayriks, ayd jhamanak klorik tasnhingamya aghjik, &s derqery calac cher nstowm, na ognowm er krpakowm, naxnakan ktronner er sosndowm, kiraki orerin araqowm er apranqnery &, chnayac och aynqan sahown, sakayn harowst er&akayowtyamb teladrvac namak֊hishocner er growm partapannerin։ Cavoq, ind mot chi pahpanvel ayd namakneric och meky։ Orqan lav kliner aystegh mej berel kisamankakan֊kisaaghjkakan ayd kocheric mi qanisy, oronq grvac ein kisaorbi koghmic, orovhet& Kolyaycheky drs&orec iren orpes och aynqan howsali xort hayr։ Avelin, im tatikic & nra aghjkanic mec janqer ein pahanjvowm irenc pghndov & poqr qanakov arcatov dramarkghy, ory baghkacac er erkow՝ meky myowsi vra shrjac titeghya apseneric, taqcnelow Kolyaychekyan՝ mshtapes caravic tanjvogh ayd varodagorci, melanxolik hayacqneric։ Miayn erb Gregory   tvin mahacav harbowxic, nranc ekamowtnery mecacan, te& och chapazanc shat, orovhet& i՞nch kareli er vatwarel tasnyot tvin։ 
 Mekowkes senyakanoc bnakarani nnjaranowm, ory varodagorci mahic heto datark er mnacel, orovhet& im mayriky djhoxqi tanjanqneric vaxenalow pattwarov chcankacav ayntegh teghapoxvel, teghavorvec Yan Bronskin՝ ayd jhamanak motavorapes qsanamya nra zarmiky, ory lqel er hayreni Bisaow qaghaqy & ir hory՝ Vincentin, orpeszi Qarthaowsi mijnakarg dproci lav avartavkayakany derqin՝ verj talov shrjanayin qaghaqi postowm ashakertowtyany, ayjhm Dancigi glxavor postatann sksi mijin dasi carayoghi karieran։ Twamprowkic baci Yany ir horaqroj bnakaran er berel namakanishneri bavakanin cavalown ir havaqacown։ Namakanishner havaqely na sksel er vagh mankakan hasakic, ayd isk pattwarov posti handep owner och miayn carayoghakan, ayl& zowt andnakan, shat hogatar verabermownq։ Manrakazm, mejqy poqr֊inch kor eritasardy ashxarhin er nerkayanowm hatweli, dvad&, gowce qich qaghcr demqov & erknagowyn achqerov, mi xosqov, liovin bavarar, orpeszi im mayry, ori tansyot tarin nor er lracel, nran siraharver։ Yanin arden ereq angam zorakochel ein zinvorakan znnman & amen angam xotanel hivandowtyan pattwarov։ Isk ayn jhamanaknerowm bolor qich te shat barekazmnery owghigh twanaparhov owgharkvowm ein depi Verden, orpeszi heto fransiakan hoghi vra haverjh horizonakan dirq yndownen, inchpes sahmanadrowtyan howyjh pertwaxos lezvov asowm er Yan Bronskin։ 
 Siravepy, ankeghc asac, petq e sksver arden namakanishneri hamategh owsowmnasirowtyownic, glowx glxi tvac aravel arjheqavor nmowshneri atamikneri znnowmic։ Sakayn ayn sksvec kam asenq, portkac, miayn erb Yanin kanchecin chorrord znnman։ Mayriks owghekcowm er nran, orovhet&, mi&nowyn e, nran petq er gnal qaghaq, & ayntegh spasowm er pahakaket pahakaxciki mot, ory hskowm er pahestnery։ Yani het oroshecin, or ays angam arden irenq petq e owgh&orven Fransia, orpeszi ayd erkri erkatov ow artwitwov harowst ody bowjhi Yani towyl krcqavandaky։ Hnaravor e, or mayrs bazmics verahashvec ashxarhazorayin hamazgesti kotwaknery & amen angam՝ tarber ardyownqnerov։ Es miangamayn karogh em patkeracnel, or cankacac hamazgesti vra kotwaknery teghakayvac en aynpes, or tvov verjin kotwaky xorhrdanshowm e Vogezovi bazmativ bardrownqneric meky, kam getaky՝ Zomen, kam Marnen։ 
 Erb chorrord angam znnman ekac tghan grete mek jham anc dowrs trav shrjanayin paretatan shqamowtqic, cac glorvec astitwanneric & ynkav Agnesi՝ aysinqn՝ im mor, paranocy, nra akanjin shshnjac ayn jhamanak shat taracvac asacvacqy․ «Och kashi, och mrowt, mi tari khetadgenq»։ Mayriks arajin angam grkec Yan Bronskown, & es vstah chem, te nran apagayowm &s vitwakvac er nowynchap erjanik linel, erb na grkowm er Yanin։ Razmakan tarineri ays patanekan siro manramasnern ind haytni chen։ Yany vatwarec ir namakanishneri havaqacowi mi masy, orpeszi hamapatasxani mayrikis havaknowtyownnerin, ory caytown artahaytac՝ hakowm owner amen gegheciki, modayiki & tankarjheqi handep, baci ayd, na henc ayd jhamanak oragir er pahowm, ory hetagayowm djhbaxtabar korav։ Tatiks, amen inchic datelov, neroghamtoren er verabervowm eritasardneri kapin՝ djhvar cher krahel, or ayd kapy dowrs er galis zowt barekamakani shrjanakneric, qani or Yan Bronskin sharownakowm er kenal Troili negh bnakaranowm։ Na dowrs ekav miayn paterazmi avartic qich anc & ayn el ayn jhamanak, erb arden hnaravor cher chnkatel omn paron Macerati goyowtyowny &, het&abar, hark eghav da xostovanel։ Mayrs, petq e karcel, verohishyal paroni het canotacav tasnowt tvi amrany, erb bowjhqroj ognakanowhi er Olivayic och herow Zilberhamer lazaretowm։ Alfred Maceraty, ory cnowndov Raynlandic er, parkac er ayntegh azdri papowk mkanneri mijacik vnasvacqov &, shnorhiv ir raynlandakan kensaxndowtyan, showtov dardav bolor qowyreri sirelin՝ chbacarelov qowyr Agnesin։ Na olor֊molor qaylowm er mijancqov, qowyreric or&e meki t&y mtac & ognowm er Qowyrik Agnesayin xohanocowm, orovhet& chapazanc shat er nra klorik demqin sazowm qowyrakan glxashory՝ dran gowmarac ayn hangamanqy, or na krqot klanvac er epel֊tapelov & karoghanowm er ir zgacmownqnery nerdnel apowrneri mej։ 
 Aroghjanalowc heto Alfred Maceraty mnac Dancigowm & anmijapes ashxatanq gtav tghtardyownaberowtyan xoshor dernarkowtyownowm՝ orpes ir raynyan dernarkowtyan nerkayacowcich։ Paterazmy gnowm er depi avarty &, arit steghcelov apaga paterazmneri hamar, jhoghovowrdy nstec xaghagh paymanagrer kazmelow, Vayqseli [ ] getaberann yndgrkogh shrjanic akasc Fogelzangic, ory Nehrowng getaki vra e, motavorapes Nogat geti erkaynqov minch& Pikely, ayntegh gnalov Vayqseli hosanqov nerq&, minch& Chatkaow, aynowhet& owghigh ankyan tak depi dax՝ minch& Shyonflis, ayntegh, agheghnad& crvelov Zaskoshinskyan pshater& antari showrj minch& Otominyan litwy, mi koghm toghnelov Materny, Ramqaown & im tatiki Bisaown & dowrs galov depi Baltik cov Klyayn֊Kaci mot՝ ayd shrjany hrchakvec Azat Dancig qaghaq & veraentarkvec Azgeri Ligayin։ Lehastany qaghaqi taracqowm stacav azat navahangist՝ Vesterplaten ir zinanocov, erkatgci tnorinowtyamb & H&eliows֊placi vrayi sepakan postatnov։ 
 Ayn jhamanak, erb Azat qaghaqi namakanishnery namakneri hamar arajarkvowm ein karmraoskegowyn hanzayakan twoxowtyan gerbi vra ar&trakani patkerov, lehery namakneri vra kpcnowm ein achqi zarnogh manowshakagowyn nkarner, oronq patkerowm ein patmowtyownner Kazimiri & Batorii masin։ 
 Yan Bronskin carayowtyan teghapoxvec Lehakan postatown։ Nra teghapoxowtyowny havasarapes nra lehakan qaghaqaciowtyowny, anspaseli er ditvowm։ Orpes pattwarneric meky, ori drdmamb na lehakan qaghaqaciowtyown yndownec, shatery hamarecin im tatiki varqagicy։ Qsan tvin, erb marshal Pilsowdskin Varshavayi tak jaxjaxec Karmir banaky, & ayd hrashqi hamar Vayqseli vra mardik, Vincent Bronskow pes, shnorhakalowtyown ein haytnowm Kowys Mariamin, isk razmakan gorci gitaknery bolor derqberowmnery veragrowm ein general Sikorskown kam general Veygandin՝ mi xosqov ayd bown lehakan taretvin im mayriky nshanvec kayserakan germanaci Macerati het։ Es owzowm em mtacel, or Anna tatiks nowynchap havanowtyown tvec ayd nshandreqin, orchap & Yany։ Na aghjkan zijec Troili vrayi nkowghayin krpaky, orn ayd yntacqowm nshanakali caghkman er hasel, inqy teghapoxvec Bisaow, ir Vincent eghbor mot, kartw asac՝ lehakan hogheri vra &, inchpes minchkolyaychekan jhamanaknerowm, ir vra vercrec baky, twakndeghi ow kartofili dashtery, erjankowtyamb hamakvac ir eghbory ynderelov aravel shat jhamanak Lehastani kowys tagowhow het shpman ow erkxosowtyan hamar, isk inqy bavararvec ir chors shrjazgestnerov ayrvogh ter&owqov ashnanayin xarowyki mot nstelow & arajva pes heraxosasyownerov andamahatvac horizoni owghghowtyamb nayelow hnaravorowtyamb։
